		name = new_sun_cult.6.a
		decrease_nsc_isolation_level = yes
	}
}

#Setup if MoH is disabled
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.7
	title = new_sun_cult.7.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.7.d
	picture = DIPLOMACY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = { }
	
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.7.a
		if = { limit = { NOT = { has_dlc = "Mandate of Heaven" } }
			#Irrliam
			F37 = {
				add_historical_friend = F40
				add_historical_friend = F43
			}
			F40 = { add_historical_friend = F37 }
			F43 = { add_historical_friend = F37 }
			#Elizna
			U05 = { add_historical_friend = F32 }
			F32 = { add_historical_friend = U05 }
			#Sareyand
			F25 = {
				add_historical_friend = U20
				add_historical_friend = F31
				add_historical_friend = F41
			}
			U20 = { add_historical_friend = F25 }
			F31 = { add_historical_friend = F25 }
			F41 = { add_historical_friend = F25 }
			#Birsartanses
			F21 = { add_historical_friend = F26 }
			F26 = { add_historical_friend = F21 }
			#Azka-Evran
			F34 = { add_historical_friend = U19 }
			U19 = { add_historical_friend = F34 }
			#Varamhar
			F42 = {
				add_historical_friend = F30
				add_historical_friend = F33
			}
			F30 = { add_historical_friend = F42 }
			F33 = { add_historical_friend = F42 }
		}
	}
}

#Lucian Carter arrives in the Drolas (Betelis province)
province_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.8
	title = new_sun_cult.8.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.8.d
	picture = DIPLOMACY_eventPicture
	goto = ROOT
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	#
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.8.a
		owner = {
			add_years_of_income = 0.1
			light_ship = ROOT		
		}
		province_event = { id = new_sun_cult.9 days = 1825 }
	}
}

#Lucian Carter 2
province_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.9
	title = new_sun_cult.9.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.9.d
	picture = DIPLOMACY_eventPicture
	goto = ROOT
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_province = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						area = inner_drolas_area
						area = outer_drolas_area
					}
					NOT = { has_province_modifier = nsc_teaching_the_one_god }
				}
				save_event_target_as = drolas_province_1
			}
			random_province = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						area = inner_drolas_area
						area = outer_drolas_area
					}
					NOT = { has_province_modifier = nsc_teaching_the_one_god }
				}
				save_event_target_as = drolas_province_2
			}
		}
	}
	
	#Leave him
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.9.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		change_religion = ravelian
		add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = "religious_zeal_at_conv" duration = 9125 }
		add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = nsc_teaching_the_one_god duration = 9125 }
		event_target:drolas_province_1 = {
			change_religion = ravelian
			add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = nsc_teaching_the_one_god duration = 9125 }
			add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = "religious_zeal_at_conv" duration = 9125 }
		}
		event_target:drolas_province_2 = {
			change_religion = ravelian
			add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = nsc_teaching_the_one_god duration = 9125 }
			add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = "religious_zeal_at_conv" duration = 9125 }
		}
		owner = { set_country_flag = nsc_lucian_carter_in_our_lands }
	}
	
	#Expel the dude
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.9.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		owner = { add_adm_power = -50 }
		change_religion = ravelian
		add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = nsc_drolas_missionaries_expelled duration = 3650 }
		event_target:drolas_province_1 = {
			change_religion = ravelian
			add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = nsc_drolas_missionaries_expelled duration = 3650 }
		}
		event_target:drolas_province_2 = {
			change_religion = ravelian
			add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = nsc_drolas_missionaries_expelled duration = 3650 }
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		owner = { set_country_flag = nsc_lucian_carter_happened }
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				religion = bulwari_sun_cult
				NOT = { capital_scope = { continent = south_america } }
				NOT = { capital_scope = { continent = north_america } }
			}
			set_country_flag = nsc_lucian_carter_happened
		}
	}
}

#Getting back the mage estate on conversion or new ruler
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.10
	title = new_sun_cult.10.t
	desc = { trigger = { religion = bulwari_sun_cult is_chosen_country = yes } desc = new_sun_cult.10.da }
	desc = { trigger = { NOT = { religion = bulwari_sun_cult } } desc = new_sun_cult.10.db }
	picture = BIG_BOOK_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = nsc_human_country_magic_prohibition
		NOT = { has_country_flag = updating_isolationism_window }
		OR = {
			NOT = { religion = bulwari_sun_cult }
			is_chosen_country = yes
		}
		NOT = { has_country_flag = nsc_teachings_szal_fazil_started }
	}
	
	#
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.10.a
		custom_tooltip = nsc_enable_mage_estate_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = mage_organization_centralized_flag
			clr_country_flag = nsc_human_country_magic_prohibition
			country_event = { id = anbennar_setup.6 days = 3 }
		}
	}
}

#---------------# Dukeldar #-----------------#
#Dukeldar start
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.15
	title = new_sun_cult.15.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.15.d
	picture = ARTWORK_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		ai = no
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.16 days = 365 random = 180 }
			set_country_flag = has_nsc_disaster
			set_variable = { which = nscDisasterScoreVar value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = totalMonthlyNscDisasterScoreVar value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = nscDisasterConversionScoreVar value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = nscDisasterBattleWonScoreVar value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = nscDisasterBattleLostScoreVar value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = nscDisasterHereticConversionsVar value = 0 }
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						religion = the_jadd
						religion = old_bulwari_sun_cult
					}
				}
				remove_province_modifier = "religious_zeal_at_conv"
				set_province_flag = dukeldar_conversion
			}
			# nsc_update_monthly_disaster_score = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.15.a
		if = { limit = { ai = no }
			add_stability = -3
			capital_scope = { spawn_rebels = { type = anti_tax_rebels size = 3 } }
		}
	}
}

#Main events
#Administration goes on strike
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.16
	title = new_sun_cult.16.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.16.d
	picture = ARTWORK_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.17 days = 365 random = 180 } }
	}
	
	#Fuck them
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.16.a
		custom_tooltip = nsc_advisors_likely_to_desert_tt
		remove_advisor_by_category = ADM
		remove_advisor_by_category = DIP
		remove_advisor_by_category = MIL
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_rebellious_administration duration = -1 desc = nsc_until_disaster_end_tt }
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_admin_on_strike duration = 365 }
		set_country_flag = nsc_administatrion_on_strike
	}
	
	#Raise pay
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.16.b
		custom_tooltip = nsc_advisors_less_likely_to_desert_tt
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_advisor_more_paid duration = -1 desc = nsc_until_disaster_end_tt }
		remove_advisor_by_category = ADM
		remove_advisor_by_category = DIP
		remove_advisor_by_category = MIL
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_rebellious_administration duration = -1 desc = nsc_until_disaster_end_tt }
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_admin_on_strike duration = 180 }
		set_country_flag = nsc_administatrion_on_strike
	}
	
	after = {
		# hidden_effect = { nsc_update_monthly_disaster_score = yes }
	}
}

#Military demand more pay
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.17
	title = new_sun_cult.17.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.17.d
	picture = ARTWORK_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.18 days = 365 random = 180 } }
	}
	
	#Refuse
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.17.a
		custom_tooltip = nsc_troops_likely_to_desert_tt
		set_country_flag = dukeldar_desertions
	}
	
	#Accept
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.17.b
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_army_more_paid duration = 3650 }
		custom_tooltip = nsc_troops_less_likely_to_desert_tt
		set_country_flag = dukeldar_desertions
	}
}

#Clergy propose a deal
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.18
	title = new_sun_cult.18.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.18.d
	picture = ARTWORK_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.19 days = 365 random = 180 } }
	}
	
	#Accept
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.18.a
		give_estate_land_share_gigantic = { estate = estate_church }
		add_estate_influence_modifier = {
			estate = estate_church
			desc = nsc_church_deal
			influence = 20
			duration = 7300
		}
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_clergy_support duration = -1 desc = nsc_until_disaster_end_tt }
	}
	
	#Refuse
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.18.b
		add_estate_loyalty = { estate = estate_church loyalty = -10 }
	}
}

#Populace protesting
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.19
	title = new_sun_cult.19.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.19.d
	picture = ARTWORK_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.20 days = 365 random = 180 }
			set_variable = { which = numRebelProvinceVar value = -12 }
			every_owned_province = { ROOT = { change_variable = { which = numRebelProvinceVar value = 1 } } }
			divide_variable = { which = numRebelProvinceVar value = 4 }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = numRebelProvinceVar value = 10 } }
				set_variable = { which = numRebelProvinceVar value = 9 }
			}
			set_variable = { which = twoThirdRebelProvinceVar which = numRebelProvinceVar }
			change_variable = { which = twoThirdRebelProvinceVar value = 1 }
			divide_variable = { which = twoThirdRebelProvinceVar value = 1.5 }
			set_variable = { which = oneThirdRebelProvinceVar which = numRebelProvinceVar }
			change_variable = { which = oneThirdRebelProvinceVar value = 1 }
			divide_variable = { which = oneThirdRebelProvinceVar value = 3 }
			
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = { is_capital = no }
				spawn_rebels = { type = anti_tax_rebels size = 3 }
				set_province_flag = dukeldar_rebellion
				while = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = {
							check_variable = { which = numRebelProvinceVar value = 1 }
							check_variable = { which = numRebelProvinceVar which = twoThirdRebelProvinceVar }
						}
					}
					random_neighbor_province = {
						limit = {
							is_capital = no
							NOT = { has_province_flag = dukeldar_rebellion }
						}
						spawn_rebels = { type = anti_tax_rebels size = 1 }
						set_province_flag = dukeldar_rebellion
					}
					ROOT = { change_variable = { which = numRebelProvinceVar value = -1 } }
				}
			}
			
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					is_capital = no
					NOT = { has_province_flag = dukeldar_rebellion }
				}
				spawn_rebels = { type = anti_tax_rebels size = 3 }
				set_province_flag = dukeldar_rebellion
				while = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = {
							check_variable = { which = numRebelProvinceVar value = 1 }
							check_variable = { which = numRebelProvinceVar which = oneThirdRebelProvinceVar }
						}
					}
					random_neighbor_province = {
						limit = {
							is_capital = no
							NOT = { has_province_flag = dukeldar_rebellion }
						}
						spawn_rebels = { type = anti_tax_rebels size = 1 }
						set_province_flag = dukeldar_rebellion
					}
					ROOT = { change_variable = { which = numRebelProvinceVar value = -1 } }
				}
			}
			
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					is_capital = no
					NOT = { has_province_flag = dukeldar_rebellion }
				}
				spawn_rebels = { type = anti_tax_rebels size = 3 }
				set_province_flag = dukeldar_rebellion
				while = {
					limit = { ROOT = { check_variable = { which = numRebelProvinceVar value = 1 } } }
					random_neighbor_province = {
						limit = {
							is_capital = no
							NOT = { has_province_flag = dukeldar_rebellion }
						}
						spawn_rebels = { type = anti_tax_rebels size = 1 }
						set_province_flag = dukeldar_rebellion
					}
					ROOT = { change_variable = { which = numRebelProvinceVar value = -1 } }
				}
			}
			
			# nsc_update_monthly_disaster_score = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.19.a
	}
}

#Nobility backs you up
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.20
	title = new_sun_cult.20.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.20.d
	picture = ARTWORK_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.21 days = 365 random = 180 } }
	}
	
	#Cool
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.20.a
		add_stability_or_adm_power = yes
		add_estate_influence_modifier = {
			estate = estate_nobles
			desc = nsc_nobility_backing
			influence = 20
			duration = 7300
		}
	}
	
	#Fuck off
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.20.b
		add_estate_loyalty = { estate = estate_nobles loyalty = -10 }
	}
}

#Pretenders
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.21
	title = new_sun_cult.21.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.21.d
	picture = ARTWORK_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { limit = { capital_scope = { region = bulwar_proper_region } }
				F39 = { save_event_target_as = bulwari_origin }
				set_saved_name = {
					key = dukedal_pretender
					type = advisor
					scope = event_target:bulwari_origin
				}
			}
			else_if = { limit = { capital_scope = { region = far_bulwar_region } }
				U20 = { save_event_target_as = surani_origin }
				set_saved_name = {
					key = dukedal_pretender
					type = advisor
					scope = event_target:surani_origin
				}
			}
			else = {
				U19 = { save_event_target_as = bahari_origin }
				set_saved_name = {
					key = dukedal_pretender
					type = advisor
					scope = event_target:bahari_origin
				}
			}
			
			set_variable = { which = numPretenderProvinceVar value = -15 }
			every_owned_province = { ROOT = { change_variable = { which = numPretenderProvinceVar value = 1 } } }
			divide_variable = { which = numPretenderProvinceVar value = 5 }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = numPretenderProvinceVar value = 7 } }
				set_variable = { which = numPretenderProvinceVar value = 6 }
			}
			set_variable = { which = twoThirdPretenderProvinceVar which = numPretenderProvinceVar }
			change_variable = { which = twoThirdPretenderProvinceVar value = 1 }
			divide_variable = { which = twoThirdPretenderProvinceVar value = 1.5 }
			set_variable = { which = oneThirdPretenderProvinceVar which = numPretenderProvinceVar }
			change_variable = { which = oneThirdPretenderProvinceVar value = 1 }
			divide_variable = { which = oneThirdPretenderProvinceVar value = 3 }
			
			capital_scope = {
				spawn_rebels = {
					size = 3
					leader = dukedal_pretender
					type = pretender_rebels
					culture = zanite
					win = yes
				}
				set_province_flag = dukeldar_pretender_province
				while = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = {
							check_variable = { which = numPretenderProvinceVar value = 1 }
							check_variable = { which = numPretenderProvinceVar which = twoThirdPretenderProvinceVar }
						}
					}
					random_neighbor_province = {
						limit = { NOT = { has_province_flag = dukeldar_pretender_province } }
						spawn_rebels = {
							size = 2
							type = pretender_rebels
							culture = zanite
							win = yes
						}
						set_province_flag = dukeldar_pretender_province
					}
					ROOT = { change_variable = { which = numPretenderProvinceVar value = -1 } }
				}
			}
			
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { controlled_by = REB }
					NOT = { has_province_flag = dukeldar_pretender_province }
				}
				spawn_rebels = {
					size = 2
					type = pretender_rebels
					culture = zanite
					win = yes
				}
				set_province_flag = dukeldar_pretender_province
				while = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = {
							check_variable = { which = numPretenderProvinceVar value = 1 }
							check_variable = { which = numPretenderProvinceVar which = oneThirdPretenderProvinceVar }
						}
					}
					random_neighbor_province = {
						limit = { NOT = { has_province_flag = dukeldar_pretender_province } }
						spawn_rebels = {
							size = 2
							type = pretender_rebels
							culture = zanite
							win = yes
						}
						set_province_flag = dukeldar_pretender_province
					}
					ROOT = { change_variable = { which = numPretenderProvinceVar value = -1 } }
				}
			}
			
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { controlled_by = REB }
					NOT = { has_province_flag = dukeldar_pretender_province }
				}
				spawn_rebels = {
					size = 2
					type = pretender_rebels
					culture = zanite
					win = yes
				}
				set_province_flag = dukeldar_pretender_province
				while = {
					limit = { ROOT = { check_variable = { which = numPretenderProvinceVar value = 1 } } }
					random_neighbor_province = {
						limit = { NOT = { has_province_flag = dukeldar_pretender_province } }
						spawn_rebels = {
							size = 2
							type = pretender_rebels
							culture = zanite
							win = yes
						}
						set_province_flag = dukeldar_pretender_province
					}
					ROOT = { change_variable = { which = numPretenderProvinceVar value = -1 } }
				}
			}
			
			# nsc_update_monthly_disaster_score = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.21.a
		add_legitimacy = -10
		add_republican_tradition = -3
		add_devotion = -10
		set_country_flag = nsc_dukeldar_pretender_spawned
	}
}

#Disaster end
#
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.26
	title = new_sun_cult.26.t
	desc = { trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = dukedal_lost } } desc = new_sun_cult.26.da }
	desc = { trigger = { has_country_flag = dukedal_lost } desc = new_sun_cult.26.db }
	picture = { trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = dukedal_lost } } picture = ARTWORK_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { has_country_flag = dukedal_lost } picture = ARTWORK_eventPicture }
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						NOT = { religion = bulwari_sun_cult }
						is_chosen_country = no
						NOT = { check_variable = { which = nscDisasterScoreVar value = 100 } }
						NOT = { has_country_flag = nsc_dukeldar_pretender_spawned }
						any_owned_province = {
							OR = {
								religion = old_bulwari_sun_cult
								religion = the_jadd
							}
						}
						num_of_rebel_controlled_provinces = 1
						num_of_rebel_armies = 1
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = dukedal_lost
			}
		}
	}
	
	#Won disaster
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.26.a
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = dukedal_lost } ai = no }
		add_stability_or_adm_power = yes
		add_stability_or_adm_power = yes
		increase_nsc_isolation_level = yes
		if = { limit = { NOT = { isolationism = 2 } }
			increase_nsc_isolation_level = yes
		}
		custom_tooltip = nsc_dukeldar_will_be_back_tt
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_army_more_paid
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_clergy_support
	}
	
	#Lost disaster
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.26.b
		trigger = { has_country_flag = dukedal_lost ai = no }
		add_prestige = -50
		custom_tooltip = nsc_dukeldar_will_be_back_tt
		#clr_country_flag = dukedal_lost
		
		clr_country_flag = locked_racial_administration
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					primary_culture = sun_elf
					primary_culture = dawn_elf
				}
			}
			if = { limit = { capital_scope = { region = far_bulwar_region } }
				change_primary_culture = surani
			}
			else_if = { limit = { capital_scope = { region = bahar_region } }
				change_primary_culture = bahari
			}
			else = {
				change_primary_culture = zanite
			}
		}
		if = { limit = { OR = { heir_culture = sun_elf heir_culture = dawn_elf } }
			kill_heir = { allow_new_heir = no }
		}
		if = { limit = { OR = { consort_culture = sun_elf consort_culture = dawn_elf } }
			remove_consort_effect = yes
		}
		if = { limit = { OR = { ruler_culture = sun_elf ruler_culture = dawn_elf } }
			kill_ruler = yes
		}
		
		if = { limit = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = human_administration } }
			clear_racial_administration = yes
			add_country_modifier = { name = restructuring_administration duration = 3650 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = human_administration duration = -1 hidden = yes }
		}
		
		if = { limit = { tag = F38 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { primary_culture = sun_elf }
					NOT = { religion = the_jadd }
					NOT = { exists = F52 }
				}
				
				change_tag = F52
				swap_non_generic_missions = yes
				hidden_effect = { restore_country_name = yes }
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = F38_mantle_of_the_conqueror }
					swap_free_idea_group = yes
				}
				lock_racial_admin = yes
				set_country_flag = formed_great_bulwar_flag
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					religion = the_jadd
					NOT = { exists = F51 }
				}
				change_tag = F51
				hidden_effect = { restore_country_name = yes }
				swap_non_generic_missions = yes
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = F38_mantle_of_the_conqueror }
					swap_free_idea_group = yes
				}
				if = { limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				add_government_reform = jadd_empire
				# if = { limit = { has_dlc = "Dharma" }
				# 	add_government_reform = jadd_nobility
				# }
				country_event = { id = jadd_empire.1 }
				set_country_flag = formed_jadd_empire_flag
			}
		}
		
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_army_more_paid
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_clergy_support
	}
	
	#AI bypass
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.26.c
		trigger = { ai = yes }
		increase_nsc_isolation_level = yes
	}
	
	after = {
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_admin_on_strike
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_advisor_more_paid
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_rebellious_administration
		set_country_flag = nsc_dukeldar_end
		clr_country_flag = has_nsc_disaster
		clr_country_flag = nsc_lost_war
		clr_country_flag = nsc_dukeldar_pretender_spawned
		clr_country_flag = nsc_administatrion_on_strike
		clr_country_flag = dukeldar_desertions
		every_owned_province = {
			clr_province_flag = dukeldar_rebellion
			clr_province_flag = dukeldar_conversion
			clr_province_flag = dukeldar_pretender_province
		}
	}
}

			set_variable = { which = nscDisasterConversionScoreVar value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = nscDisasterBattleWonScoreVar value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = nscDisasterBattleLostScoreVar value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = nscDisasterHereticConversionsVar value = 0 }
			# nsc_update_monthly_disaster_score = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.27.a
		if = { limit = { ai = no }
			add_stability = -3
			capital_scope = { spawn_rebels = { type = sun_elf_loyalists_rebels size = 3 } }
			add_estate_loyalty = { estate = estate_nobles loyalty = -20 }
			add_estate_loyalty = { estate = estate_church loyalty = -20 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.30
	title = new_sun_cult.30.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.30.d
	picture = ARTWORK_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_province_flag = dinam_elutur_sun_elf_loyalists_rebels } }
				save_event_target_as = dinam_elutur_clergy_rebels_1
				random_neighbor_province = {
					save_event_target_as = dinam_elutur_clergy_rebels_2
				}
				random_neighbor_province = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_province_flag = dinam_elutur_sun_elf_loyalists_rebels } }
					save_event_target_as = dinam_elutur_clergy_rebels_2
				}
				random_neighbor_province = {
					limit = { NOT = { province_id = event_target:dinam_elutur_clergy_rebels_2 } }
					save_event_target_as = dinam_elutur_clergy_rebels_3
				}
				random_neighbor_province = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_province_flag = dinam_elutur_sun_elf_loyalists_rebels }
						NOT = { province_id = event_target:dinam_elutur_clergy_rebels_2 }
					}
					save_event_target_as = dinam_elutur_clergy_rebels_3
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.31 days = 365 random = 30 }
		}
	}
	
	#Remove their privileges
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.30.a
		custom_tooltip = nsc_dinam_elutur_less_powerful_clergy_tt
		set_country_flag = dinam_elutur_less_powerful_clergy
		# remove_estate_privilege = estate_church_independent_clergy
		add_estate_loyalty = { estate = estate_church loyalty = -20 }
		reduce_stability_or_adm_power = yes
		event_target:dinam_elutur_clergy_rebels_1 = {
			set_province_flag = dinam_elutur_sun_elf_loyalists_rebels
			spawn_rebels = {
				type = sun_elf_loyalists_rebels
				size = 2
			}
		}
		event_target:dinam_elutur_clergy_rebels_2 = {
			set_province_flag = dinam_elutur_sun_elf_loyalists_rebels
			spawn_rebels = {
				type = sun_elf_loyalists_rebels
				size = 1
			}
		}
		event_target:dinam_elutur_clergy_rebels_3 = {
			set_province_flag = dinam_elutur_sun_elf_loyalists_rebels
			spawn_rebels = {
				type = sun_elf_loyalists_rebels
				size = 1
			}
		}
	}
	
	#Let them be
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.30.b
		custom_tooltip = nsc_dinam_elutur_powerful_clergy_tt
	}
}

#Sun elf loyalist protest
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.33
	title = new_sun_cult.33.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.33.d
	picture = ARTWORK_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.34 days = 365 random = 30 }
			set_variable = { which = numRebelProvinceVar value = -12 }
			every_owned_province = { ROOT = { change_variable = { which = numRebelProvinceVar value = 1 } } }
			divide_variable = { which = numRebelProvinceVar value = 4 }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = numRebelProvinceVar value = 10 } }
				set_variable = { which = numRebelProvinceVar value = 9 }
			}
			set_variable = { which = twoThirdRebelProvinceVar which = numRebelProvinceVar }
			change_variable = { which = twoThirdRebelProvinceVar value = 1 }
			divide_variable = { which = twoThirdRebelProvinceVar value = 1.5 }
			set_variable = { which = oneThirdRebelProvinceVar which = numRebelProvinceVar }
			change_variable = { which = oneThirdRebelProvinceVar value = 1 }
			divide_variable = { which = oneThirdRebelProvinceVar value = 3 }
			
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = { is_capital = no }
				spawn_rebels = { type = sun_elf_loyalists_rebels size = 3 }
				set_province_flag = dinam_elutur_rebellion
				while = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = {
							check_variable = { which = numRebelProvinceVar value = 1 }
							check_variable = { which = numRebelProvinceVar which = twoThirdRebelProvinceVar }
						}
					}
					random_neighbor_province = {
						limit = {
							is_capital = no
							NOT = { has_province_flag = dinam_elutur_rebellion }
						}
						spawn_rebels = { type = sun_elf_loyalists_rebels size = 1 }
						set_province_flag = dinam_elutur_rebellion
					}
					ROOT = { change_variable = { which = numRebelProvinceVar value = -1 } }
				}
			}
			
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					is_capital = no
					NOT = { has_province_flag = dinam_elutur_rebellion }
				}
				spawn_rebels = { type = sun_elf_loyalists_rebels size = 2 }
				set_province_flag = dinam_elutur_rebellion
				while = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = {
							check_variable = { which = numRebelProvinceVar value = 1 }
							check_variable = { which = numRebelProvinceVar which = oneThirdRebelProvinceVar }
						}
					}
					random_neighbor_province = {
						limit = {
							is_capital = no
							NOT = { has_province_flag = dinam_elutur_rebellion }
						}
						spawn_rebels = { type = sun_elf_loyalists_rebels size = 1 }
						set_province_flag = dinam_elutur_rebellion
					}
					ROOT = { change_variable = { which = numRebelProvinceVar value = -1 } }
				}
			}
			
			# nsc_update_monthly_disaster_score = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.33.a
	}
}

#Pretenders
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.34
	title = new_sun_cult.34.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.34.d
	picture = ARTWORK_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			
			set_variable = { which = numPretenderProvinceVar value = -15 }
			every_owned_province = { ROOT = { change_variable = { which = numPretenderProvinceVar value = 1 } } }
			divide_variable = { which = numPretenderProvinceVar value = 5 }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = numPretenderProvinceVar value = 7 } }
				set_variable = { which = numPretenderProvinceVar value = 6 }
			}
			set_variable = { which = twoThirdPretenderProvinceVar which = numPretenderProvinceVar }
			change_variable = { which = twoThirdPretenderProvinceVar value = 1 }
			divide_variable = { which = twoThirdPretenderProvinceVar value = 1.5 }
			set_variable = { which = oneThirdPretenderProvinceVar which = numPretenderProvinceVar }
			change_variable = { which = oneThirdPretenderProvinceVar value = 1 }
			divide_variable = { which = oneThirdPretenderProvinceVar value = 3 }
			
			if = { limit = { capital_scope = { OR = { continent = north_america continent = south_america } } }
				H67 = { save_event_target_as = aelantiri_origin }
				set_saved_name = {
					key = dinam_elutur_pretender
					type = advisor
					scope = event_target:aelantiri_origin
				}
			}
			else = {
				F34 = { save_event_target_as = bulwari_origin }
				set_saved_name = {
					key = dinam_elutur_pretender
					type = advisor
					scope = event_target:bulwari_origin
				}
			}
			
			capital_scope = {
				if = { limit = { OR = { continent = north_america continent = south_america } }
					spawn_rebels = {
						size = 3
						leader = dinam_elutur_pretender
						type = pretender_rebels
						culture = dawn_elf
						win = yes
					}
				}
				else = {
					spawn_rebels = {
						size = 3
						leader = dinam_elutur_pretender
						type = pretender_rebels
						culture = sun_elf
						win = yes
					}
				}
				set_province_flag = dinam_elutur_pretender_province
				while = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = {
							check_variable = { which = numPretenderProvinceVar value = 1 }
							check_variable = { which = numPretenderProvinceVar which = twoThirdPretenderProvinceVar }
						}
					}
					random_neighbor_province = {
						limit = { NOT = { has_province_flag = dinam_elutur_pretender_province } }
						spawn_rebels = {
							size = 2
							type = pretender_rebels
							culture = sun_elf
							win = yes
						}
						set_province_flag = dinam_elutur_pretender_province
					}
					ROOT = { change_variable = { which = numPretenderProvinceVar value = -1 } }
				}
			}
			
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { controlled_by = REB }
					NOT = { has_province_flag = dinam_elutur_pretender_province }
				}
				spawn_rebels = {
					size = 2
					type = pretender_rebels
					culture = sun_elf
					win = yes
				}
				set_province_flag = dinam_elutur_pretender_province
				while = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = {
							check_variable = { which = numPretenderProvinceVar value = 1 }
							check_variable = { which = numPretenderProvinceVar which = oneThirdPretenderProvinceVar }
						}
					}
					random_neighbor_province = {
						limit = { NOT = { has_province_flag = dinam_elutur_pretender_province } }
						spawn_rebels = {
							size = 2
							type = pretender_rebels
							culture = sun_elf
							win = yes
						}
						set_province_flag = dinam_elutur_pretender_province
					}
					ROOT = { change_variable = { which = numPretenderProvinceVar value = -1 } }
				}
			}
			
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { controlled_by = REB }
					NOT = { has_province_flag = dinam_elutur_pretender_province }
				}
				spawn_rebels = {
					size = 2
					type = pretender_rebels
					culture = sun_elf
					win = yes
				}
				set_province_flag = dinam_elutur_pretender_province
				while = {
					limit = { ROOT = { check_variable = { which = numPretenderProvinceVar value = 1 } } }
					random_neighbor_province = {
						limit = { NOT = { has_province_flag = dinam_elutur_pretender_province } }
						spawn_rebels = {
							size = 2
							type = pretender_rebels
							culture = sun_elf
							win = yes
						}
						set_province_flag = dinam_elutur_pretender_province
					}
					ROOT = { change_variable = { which = numPretenderProvinceVar value = -1 } }
				}
			}
			
			# nsc_update_monthly_disaster_score = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.34.a
		add_legitimacy = -10
		add_republican_tradition = -3
		add_devotion = -10
		set_country_flag = nsc_dinam_elutur_pretender_spawned
	}
}

#Administrator fucking off
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.37
	title = new_sun_cult.37.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.37.d
	picture = ARTWORK_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = nsc_administatrion_on_strike
		has_advisor = yes
	}
	
	#Do everything to make them to stay
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.37.a
		if = { limit = { employed_advisor = { category = ADM } }
			add_adm_power = -50
		}
		if = { limit = { employed_advisor = { category = DIP } }
			add_dip_power = -50
		}
		if = { limit = { employed_advisor = { category = MIL } }
			add_mil_power = -50
		}
	}
	
	#Try to make them to stay
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.37.b
		if = { limit = { employed_advisor = { category = ADM } }
			add_adm_power = -25
			random = {
				chance = 50
				remove_advisor_by_category = ADM
			}
		}
		if = { limit = { employed_advisor = { category = DIP } }
			add_dip_power = -25
			random = {
				chance = 50
				remove_advisor_by_category = DIP
			}
		}
		if = { limit = { employed_advisor = { category = MIL } }
			add_mil_power = -25
			random = {
				chance = 50
				remove_advisor_by_category = MIL
			}
		}
	}
	
	#Fuck 'em
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.37.c
		if = { limit = { employed_advisor = { category = ADM } }
			remove_advisor_by_category = ADM
		}
		if = { limit = { employed_advisor = { category = DIP } }
			remove_advisor_by_category = DIP
		}
		if = { limit = { employed_advisor = { category = MIL } }
			remove_advisor_by_category = MIL
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		# nsc_update_monthly_disaster_score = yes
	}
}

#Disaster end
#
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.39
	title = new_sun_cult.39.t
	desc = { trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = dinam_elutur_lost } } desc = new_sun_cult.39.da }
	desc = { trigger = { has_country_flag = dinam_elutur_lost } desc = new_sun_cult.39.db }
	picture = { trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = dinam_elutur_lost } } picture = ARTWORK_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { has_country_flag = dinam_elutur_lost } picture = ARTWORK_eventPicture }
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						NOT = { religion = bulwari_sun_cult }
						ruler_culture = sun_elf
						ruler_culture = dawn_elf
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = dinam_elutur_lost
			}
		}
	}
	
	#Won disaster
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.39.a
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = dinam_elutur_lost } ai = no }
		add_stability_or_adm_power = yes
		add_stability_or_adm_power = yes
		decrease_nsc_isolation_level = yes
		if = { limit = { isolationism = 3 }
			decrease_nsc_isolation_level = yes
		}
		custom_tooltip = nsc_dinam_elutur_will_be_back_tt
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_army_more_paid
	}
	
	#Lost disaster
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.39.b
		trigger = { has_country_flag = dinam_elutur_lost ai = no }
		add_prestige = -50
		custom_tooltip = nsc_dinam_elutur_will_be_back_tt
		clr_country_flag = dinam_elutur_lost
		clr_country_flag = locked_racial_administration
		if = { limit = { capital_scope = { OR = { continent = north_america continent = south_america } } }
			change_primary_culture = dawn_elf
		}
		else = {
			change_primary_culture = sun_elf
			if = { limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
				change_government = monarchy
			}
			add_government_reform = phoenix_akalate
		}
		if = { limit = { has_heir = yes NOT = { heir_culture = sun_elf } NOT = { heir_culture = dawn_elf } }
			kill_heir = { allow_new_heir = no }
		}
		if = { limit = { has_consort = yes NOT = { consort_culture = sun_elf } NOT = { consort_culture = dawn_elf } }
			remove_consort_effect = yes
		}
		if = { limit = { NOT = { ruler_culture = sun_elf } NOT = { ruler_culture = dawn_elf } }
			kill_ruler = yes
		}
		if = { limit = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = elven_administration } }
			clear_racial_administration = yes
			add_country_modifier = { name = restructuring_administration duration = 3650 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = elven_administration duration = -1 hidden = yes }
		}
		set_country_flag = locked_racial_administration
	
		if = { limit = { tag = F52 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					religion = bulwari_sun_cult
					NOT = { exists = F38 }
				}
				change_tag = F38
				hidden_effect = { restore_country_name = yes }
				swap_non_generic_missions = yes
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = F52_independent_judicial_system }
					swap_free_idea_group = yes
				}
				set_country_flag = restored_phoenix_empire_flag
				lock_racial_admin = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					religion = the_jadd
					NOT = { exists = F51 }
				}
				change_tag = F51
				hidden_effect = { restore_country_name = yes }
				swap_non_generic_missions = yes
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = F52_independent_judicial_system }
					swap_free_idea_group = yes
				}
				if = { limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				add_government_reform = jadd_empire
				# if = { limit = { has_dlc = "Dharma" }
				# 	add_government_reform = jadd_nobility
				# }
				country_event = { id = jadd_empire.1 }
				set_country_flag = formed_jadd_empire_flag
			}
		}
		
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_army_more_paid
	}
	
	#AI bypass
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.39.c
		trigger = { ai = yes }
		decrease_nsc_isolation_level = yes
	}
	
	after = {
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_admin_on_strike
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_advisor_more_paid
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_rebellious_administration
		set_country_flag = nsc_dinam_elutur_end
		clr_country_flag = has_nsc_disaster
		clr_country_flag = nsc_dinam_elutur_pretender_spawned
		clr_country_flag = nsc_administatrion_on_strike
		clr_country_flag = dinam_elutur_desertions
		clr_country_flag = dinam_elutur_angry_nobles
		clr_country_flag = dinam_elutur_less_angry_nobles
		clr_country_flag = dinam_elutur_less_powerful_clergy 
		every_owned_province = {
			clr_province_flag = dinam_elutur_rebellion
			clr_province_flag = dinam_elutur_pretender_province
			clr_province_flag = dinam_elutur_nobles_demands 
			clr_province_flag = dinam_elutur_sun_elf_loyalists_rebels
		}
	}
}

#The Decades of Devastation
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.49
	title = new_sun_cult.49.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.49.d
	picture = FAMINE_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = nsc_bulwar_under_threat_active
			country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.51 days = 30 }
			if = { limit = { ai = no }
				add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_bulwar_under_threat duration = -1 desc = nsc_until_incident_end_tt }
			}
			else = {
				add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_bulwar_under_threat_ai duration = -1 }
			}
			add_war_exhaustion = 5
			#gelkalis stuff
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = F21
					F26 = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				}

country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.59
	title = new_sun_cult.59.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.59.d
	picture = CITY_VIEW_eventPicture

	trigger = { has_country_flag = nsc_pledge }
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = { culture_group = bulwari }
				set_province_flag = nsc_mayor_target
				save_event_target_as = nsc_mayor_target_1
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					culture_group = bulwari
					NOT = { has_province_flag = nsc_mayor_target }
				}
				set_province_flag = nsc_mayor_target
				save_event_target_as = nsc_mayor_target_2
			}
		}
	}
	
	#Hell no
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.59.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 33
			modifier = { factor = 0.1 NOT = { manpower = 1 } }
			modifier = { factor = 0.1 is_at_war = yes }
			modifier = { factor = 0.75 incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_bulwar_under_threat value = 2 } }
		}
		custom_tooltip = nsc_chosen_role_up_tt
		add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_bulwar_under_threat value = 1 }
		event_target:nsc_mayor_target_1 = {
			spawn_rebels = { type = particularist_rebels size = 1 }
			add_unrest = 10
		}
		event_target:nsc_mayor_target_2 = {
			spawn_rebels = { type = particularist_rebels size = 1 }
			add_unrest = 10
		}
	}
	
	#Ok
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.59.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 66
			modifier = { factor = 0.75 NOT = { incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_bulwar_under_threat value = -1 } } }
			modifier = { factor = 0.75 NOT = { incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_bulwar_under_threat value = -2 } } }
			modifier = { factor = 0.1 tag = F25 } #Sareyand are supremacists
		}
		custom_tooltip = nsc_chosen_role_down_tt
		add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_bulwar_under_threat value = -1 }
		event_target:nsc_mayor_target_1 = {
			add_local_autonomy = 25
			add_unrest = -5
		}
		event_target:nsc_mayor_target_2 = {
			add_local_autonomy = 25
			add_unrest = -5
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.60 days = 305 random = 120 }
	}
}

	id = new_sun_cult.62
	title = new_sun_cult.62.t
	desc = { trigger = { check_variable = { which = TotalUnrestVar value = 5 } } desc = new_sun_cult.62.da }
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { which = TotalUnrestVar value = 5 } }
			check_variable = { which = TotalUnrestVar value = 1 }
		}
		desc = new_sun_cult.62.db
	}
	desc = { trigger = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = TotalUnrestVar value = 1 } } } desc = new_sun_cult.62.dc }
	picture = COURT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = { has_country_flag = nsc_pledge }
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = { nsc_calculate_unrest_percentage = yes }
	}
	
	#Massive fail
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.62.a
		trigger = { OR = { ai = yes check_variable = { which = TotalUnrestVar value = 5 } } } #ai cheats
		add_legitimacy = -10
	}
	
	#Kinda worked
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.62.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { which = TotalUnrestVar value = 5 } }
			check_variable = { which = TotalUnrestVar value = 1 }
			ai = no
		}
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_flustered_populace duration = -1 desc = nsc_until_incident_end_tt }
	}
	
	#Great success
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.62.c
		trigger = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = TotalUnrestVar value = 1 } } ai = no }
		add_stability_or_adm_power = yes
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_appeased_populace duration = -1 desc = nsc_until_incident_end_tt }
	}
	
	after = {
		every_owned_province = {
			clr_province_flag = nsc_mayor_target
			clr_province_flag = nsc_merchant_target
			clr_province_flag = nsc_peasant_target
		}
		clr_country_flag = nsc_reining_in_populace
		set_country_flag = nsc_populace_over
	}
}

#Appease your vassals menu
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.63
	title = new_sun_cult.63.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.63.d
	picture = LIBERUM_VETO_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = { has_country_flag = nsc_pledge }
	
	#reduce taxes
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.63.a
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = nsc_lowered_vassal_levies } }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = { factor = 0 all_subject_country = { NOT = { liberty_desire = 50 } } }
		}
		custom_tooltip = nsc_chosen_role_down_tt
		add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_bulwar_under_threat value = -1 }
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_lowered_vassal_levies duration = 3650 }
		every_subject_country = {
			add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_lowered_vassal_levies_vassal duration = 3650 }
		}
		clr_country_flag = nsc_appeasing_vassals
	}
	
	#reduce troops
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.63.b
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = nsc_lowered_vassal_troops } }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = { factor = 0 all_subject_country = { NOT = { liberty_desire = 50 } } }
		}
		custom_tooltip = nsc_chosen_role_down_tt
		add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_bulwar_under_threat value = -1 }
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_lowered_vassal_troops duration = 3650 }
		every_subject_country = {
			add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_lowered_vassal_troops_vassal duration = 3650 }
		}
		clr_country_flag = nsc_appeasing_vassals
	}
	
	#sun elf propaganda
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.63.c
		trigger = {
			num_of_missionaries = 1
			any_subject_country = {
				religion = bulwari_sun_cult
				NOT = { isolationism = 4 }
			}
			has_dlc = "Mandate of Heaven"
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = { factor = 0 all_subject_country = { NOT = { liberty_desire = 50 } } }
			modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { has_country_modifier = nsc_lowered_vassal_levies } }
			modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { has_country_modifier = nsc_lowered_vassal_troops } }
		}
		country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.64 }
	}
	
	#Go back
	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		name = new_sun_cult.63.e
		highlight = yes
		if = { limit = { ai = yes }
			add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_ai_took_vassal_decision duration = 1825 hidden = yes }
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		clr_country_flag = nsc_appeasing_vassals
	}
}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = { factor = 0 any_subject_country = { has_country_flag = influenceable_vassal_1_@ROOT NOT = { liberty_desire = 50 } } }
			modifier = { factor = 0 any_subject_country = { has_country_flag = influenceable_vassal_6_@ROOT ai = no } }

#Overlord has propaganded us
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.66
	title = new_sun_cult.66.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.66.d
	picture = CORRUPTION_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_subject_of = FROM
		has_country_flag = nsc_influenced_vassal_@FROM
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = nsc_propaganda_fail }
	}
	
	#Tricky bastards
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.66.a
		if = { limit = { religion = bulwari_sun_cult has_dlc = "Mandate of Heaven" }
			increase_nsc_isolation_level = yes
		}
		else = {
			add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_influenced_vassal duration = 3650 }
		}
	}
}

#Propaganda over
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.67
	title = new_sun_cult.67.t
	desc = { trigger = { FROM = { exists = yes NOT = { has_country_flag = nsc_propaganda_fail } } } desc = new_sun_cult.67.da }
	desc = { trigger = { FROM = { OR = { exists = no has_country_flag = nsc_propaganda_fail } } } desc = new_sun_cult.67.db }
	picture = CORRUPTION_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				exists = no
				has_country_flag = nsc_influenced_vassal_@ROOT
			}
		}
	}
	
	#Success
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.67.a
		trigger = { FROM = { exists = yes NOT = { has_country_flag = nsc_propaganda_fail } } }
		nsc_remove_influencing_vassal_modifier = yes
		FROM = { clr_country_flag = nsc_influenced_vassal_@ROOT }
	}
	
	#Failure
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.67.b
		trigger = { FROM = { OR = { exists = no has_country_flag = nsc_propaganda_fail } } }
		nsc_remove_influencing_vassal_modifier = yes
		FROM = {
			clr_country_flag = nsc_influenced_vassal_@ROOT
			clr_country_flag = nsc_propaganda_fail
		}
	}
}

		custom_tooltip = nsc_faster_army_reforms_tt

		name = new_sun_cult.68.c
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }

	}
}

#Tactics
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.69
	title = new_sun_cult.69.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.69.d
	picture = LAND_MILITARY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Side with the old guard - defensive tactics
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.69.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 33 }
		custom_tooltip = nsc_chosen_role_up_tt
		add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_bulwar_under_threat value = 1 }
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_defensive_tactics duration = 3650 }
	}
	
	#Side with the vanguard - mobile warfare
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.69.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 33 }
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_mobility_tactics duration = 3650 }
	}
	
	#Side with the humans - mass assault
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.69.c
		ai_chance = { factor = 33 }
		custom_tooltip = nsc_chosen_role_down_tt
		add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_bulwar_under_threat value = -1 }
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_assault_tactics duration = 3650 }
	}
	
	after = {
		if = { limit = { has_country_modifier = nsc_fast_reforms }
			country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.70 days = 180 random = 120 }
		}
		else = {
			country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.70 days = 365 random = 240 }
		}
	}
}

	picture = TRADEGOODS_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			OR = {
				is_subject_of_type = vassal
				is_subject_of_type = march
			}
		}
	}
	
	#Ok

		name = new_sun_cult.74.a

			factor = 67

		}
		FROM = {
			set_country_flag = nsc_accepted_demands
			country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.75 days = 1 }
		}
	}
	
	#Lol no
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.74.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 33 }
		FROM = {
			set_country_flag = nsc_lol_no
			country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.75 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.77
	title = new_sun_cult.77.t
	desc = { trigger = { check_variable = { which = ScoreVar value = 100 } } desc = new_sun_cult.77.da }
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { which = ScoreVar value = 100 } }
			OR = {
				check_variable = { which = ScoreVar value = 66 }
				ai = yes
			}
		}
		desc = new_sun_cult.77.db
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { which = ScoreVar value = 66 } }
			check_variable = { which = ScoreVar value = 33 }
			ai = no
		}
		desc = new_sun_cult.77.dc
	}
	desc = { trigger = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = ScoreVar value = 33 } } ai = no } desc = new_sun_cult.77.de }
	picture = { trigger = { check_variable = { which = ScoreVar value = 100 } } picture = COURT_eventPicture }

			NOT = { check_variable = { which = ScoreVar value = 100 } }
			OR = {
				check_variable = { which = ScoreVar value = 66 }

			}
		}
		picture = COURT_eventPicture
	}

		}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			nsc_calculate_pledge_score = yes
			set_country_flag = had_nsc_incident_flag

				limit = {
					tag = F21
					F26 = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				}

			}
		}
	}
	
	#Massive Success
	option = {

		trigger = { check_variable = { which = ScoreVar value = 100 } }
		end_incident = incident_bulwar_under_threat
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_pledge_great_success duration = 9125 }
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_bulwar_under_threat
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_bulwar_under_threat_ai
		if = { limit = { incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_bulwar_under_threat value = 3 } } #max -9
			custom_tooltip = nsc_choices_impact_level_tt
			increase_nsc_isolation_level = yes
		}
		else_if = { limit = { NOT = { incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_bulwar_under_threat value = -2 } } } #min +12
			custom_tooltip = nsc_choices_impact_level_tt
			decrease_nsc_isolation_level = yes
		}
		set_country_flag = birsartanses_pledge_good
	}
	
	#Success
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.77.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { which = ScoreVar value = 100 } }
			OR = {
				check_variable = { which = ScoreVar value = 66 }
				ai = yes	#ai cheats
			}
		}
		end_incident = incident_bulwar_under_threat
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_pledge_successful duration = 3650 }
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_bulwar_under_threat
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_bulwar_under_threat_ai
		if = { limit = { incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_bulwar_under_threat value = 3 } } #max -9
			custom_tooltip = nsc_choices_impact_level_tt
			increase_nsc_isolation_level = yes
		}
		else_if = { limit = { NOT = { incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_bulwar_under_threat value = -2 } } } #min +12
			custom_tooltip = nsc_choices_impact_level_tt
			decrease_nsc_isolation_level = yes
		}
		set_country_flag = birsartanses_pledge_good
	}
	
	#Partial success
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.77.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { which = ScoreVar value = 66 } }
			check_variable = { which = ScoreVar value = 33 }

		end_incident = incident_bulwar_under_threat
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_bulwar_under_threat

			custom_tooltip = nsc_choices_impact_level_tt
			increase_nsc_isolation_level = yes
		}

	}
	
	#Failure
	option = {

			custom_tooltip = nsc_choices_impact_level_tt
			decrease_nsc_isolation_level = yes
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		clr_country_flag = nsc_bulwar_under_threat_active
		clr_country_flag = active_nsc_incident_flag
		clr_country_flag = nsc_pledge
		clr_country_flag = nsc_admin_over
		clr_country_flag = nsc_populace_over
		clr_country_flag = nsc_army_over
		clr_country_flag = nsc_appeasing_vassals
		clr_country_flag = nsc_reforming_army
		clr_country_flag = nsc_ai_took_vassal_decision
		clr_country_flag = nsc_pledge_menu
		clr_country_flag = nsc_ai_pledge_menu
		clr_country_flag = azka_evran_gathering_army
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_admin_reformed
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_admin_kinda_reformed
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_flustered_populace
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_appeased_populace
		if = { limit = { NOT = { any_known_country = { has_country_flag = nsc_bulwar_under_threat_active } } }
			6106 = { remove_province_triggered_modifier = bulwar_incident_daily_pulse }
		}
	}

country_event = {

		}
	}
	
	#send a bit delegation
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.126.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = { factor = 1.5 has_opinion = { who = F37 value = 50 } }
			modifier = { factor = 1.5 has_opinion = { who = F37 value = 100 } }
			modifier = { factor = 2 alliance_with = F37 }
			modifier = { factor = 100 vassal_of = F37 }
			modifier = { factor = 0 is_rival = F37 }
			modifier = { factor = 0 tag = U05 } #Elizna doesn't give a shit
		}
		custom_tooltip = nsc_increase_unity_tt
		add_years_of_income = -0.3
		add_prestige = 10
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { limit = { is_chosen_country = yes } #sun elf choices count more
				REB = {
					change_variable = { which = nscTempUnityVar value = 2 }
					change_variable = { which = nscTotalChoicesVar value = 2 }
				}
			}
			else = {
				REB = {
					change_variable = { which = nscTempUnityVar value = 1 }
					change_variable = { which = nscTotalChoicesVar value = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	#send a medium delegation
	option = {

			modifier = { factor = 0 tag = U05 } #Elizna doesn't give a shit
		}

			}
			else = {
				REB = { change_variable = { which = nscTotalChoicesVar value = 1 } }
			}
		}
	}
	
	#Send a small delegation
	option = {

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = { factor = 0.75 has_opinion = { who = F37 value = 50 } }
			modifier = { factor = 0.75 has_opinion = { who = F37 value = 100 } }
			modifier = { factor = 0.5 alliance_with = F37 }
			modifier = { factor = 0 vassal_of = F37 }

		}

#Council Start
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.127
	title = new_sun_cult.127.t
	desc = { trigger = { check_variable = { which = nscTempUnityVar value = 33 } } desc = new_sun_cult.127.da } #everyone came to the party !
	desc = {																									#the expected people came
		trigger = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { which = nscTempUnityVar value = 33 } } 
			check_variable = { which = nscTempUnityVar value = -33 }
		}
		desc = new_sun_cult.127.db
	}
	desc = { trigger = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = nscTempUnityVar value = -33 } } } desc = new_sun_cult.127.dc } #they didn't respect our autorita !
	picture = { trigger = { check_variable = { which = nscTempUnityVar value = 33 } } picture = REFORM_eventPicture }
	picture = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { which = nscTempUnityVar value = 33 } } 
			check_variable = { which = nscTempUnityVar value = -33 }
		}
		picture = PIETY_eventPicture
	}
	picture = { trigger = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = nscTempUnityVar value = -33 } } } picture = RAMADAN_eventPicture }
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			REB = {
				if = { limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = nsc_ratio_effect_applied } }
					set_country_flag = nsc_ratio_effect_applied
					divide_variable = { which = nscTempUnityVar which = nscTotalChoicesVar }
					multiply_variable = { which = nscTempUnityVar value = 100 }
					change_variable = { which = nscUnityVar which = nscTempUnityVar }
				}
			}
			#triggering next debate
			if = { limit = { tag = F37 } 								#First Irrliam votes
				country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.128 days = 150 }
			}
			else_if = { limit = { is_vassal = no }						#Then independent countries
				country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.128 days = 300 }
			}
			else = {													#Then vassals
				country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.128 days = 450 }
			}
			country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.129 days = 600 }		#Results
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.127.a
		if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = nscTempUnityVar value = 33 } }
			add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_big_council duration = -1 desc = nsc_until_incident_end_tt }
		}
		else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = nscTempUnityVar value = -33 } }
			add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_medium_council duration = -1 desc = nsc_until_incident_end_tt }
		}
		else = {
			add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_small_council duration = -1 desc = nsc_until_incident_end_tt }
		}
	}
}

			REB = {
				if = { limit = { has_country_flag = nsc_ratio_effect_applied }
					nsc_init_choice_variables_effect = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	#god kings
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.128.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = { factor = 0.1 NOT = { isolationism = 4 } }
			modifier = { #loyal vassals have to pick the same option as their overlords
				factor = 0
				is_vassal = yes
				NOT = { liberty_desire = 50 }
				NOT = { overlord = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_a } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3 #simping for Irrliam
				F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_a }
				alliance_with = F37
			}
			modifier = { 
				factor = 2
				F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_a }
				has_opinion = { who = F37 value = 100 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0 #Elizna trolling
				F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_a }
				tag = U05 
			}
		}
		
		if = { limit = { F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_a } } #Increasing unity if picking the same option as Irrliam
			custom_tooltip = nsc_irrliam_option_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				if = { limit = { is_chosen_country = yes } #Elf choices count more
					REB = { change_variable = { which = nscIrrliamChoicesVar value = 2 } }
				}
				else = {
					REB = { change_variable = { which = nscIrrliamChoicesVar value = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { limit = { is_chosen_country = yes } #Elf choices count more
				REB = { change_variable = { which = nscChoiceAVar value = 2 } }
			}
			else = {
				REB = { change_variable = { which = nscChoiceAVar value = 1 } }
			}
			set_country_flag = nsc_choice_a
		}
		if = { limit = { NOT = { isolationism = 4 } } #moving toward an outcome raising the chosen's role if level < 4
			if = { limit = { isolationism = 3 }
				custom_tooltip = nsc_chosen_role_up_tt
				add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_death_of_taelarios value = 1 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_differing_opinion duration = 3650 }
			}
			else = {
				custom_tooltip = nsc_much_chosen_role_up_tt
				add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_death_of_taelarios value = 2 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_big_differing_opinion duration = 3650 }
			}
		}
		else = { #bonus for picking the option corresponding to your chosen's role level
			add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_congruent_opinion duration = 3650 }
		}
	}
	
	#unquestionable rulers
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.128.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				NOT = { isolationism = 3 }

			}

			}

			}

				F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_b }
				has_opinion = { who = F37 value = 100 }
			}

			}

					REB = { change_variable = { which = nscIrrliamChoicesVar value = 2 } }
				}
				else = {

			custom_tooltip = nsc_irrliam_option_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				if = { limit = { is_chosen_country = yes } #Elf choices count more
					REB = { change_variable = { which = nscIrrliamChoicesVar value = 2 } }
				}
				else = {
					REB = { change_variable = { which = nscIrrliamChoicesVar value = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { limit = { is_chosen_country = yes } #Elf choices count more
				REB = { change_variable = { which = nscChoiceCVar value = 2 } }
			}
			else = {
				REB = { change_variable = { which = nscChoiceCVar value = 1 } }
			}
			set_country_flag = nsc_choice_c
		}
		if = { limit = { NOT = { isolationism = 2 } } #moving toward an outcome raising the chosen's role if level < 2
			if = { limit = { isolationism = 1 }
				custom_tooltip = nsc_chosen_role_up_tt
				add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_death_of_taelarios value = 1 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_differing_opinion duration = 3650 }
			}
			else = {
				custom_tooltip = nsc_much_chosen_role_up_tt
				add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_death_of_taelarios value = 2 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_big_differing_opinion duration = 3650 }
			}
		}
		else_if = { limit = { isolationism = 3 } #moving toward an outcome lowering the chosen's role if level > 2
			if = { limit = { isolationism = 4 }
				custom_tooltip = nsc_much_chosen_role_down_tt
				add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_death_of_taelarios value = -2 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_big_differing_opinion duration = 3650 }
			}
			else = {
				custom_tooltip = nsc_chosen_role_down_tt
				add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_death_of_taelarios value = -1 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_differing_opinion duration = 3650 }
			}
		}
		else = { #bonus for picking the option corresponding to your chosen's role level
			add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_congruent_opinion duration = 3650 }
		}
	}
	
	#guides
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.128.e
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				NOT = { isolationism = 1 }
				isolationism = 2
			}
			modifier = { #loyal vassals have to pick the same option as their overlords
				factor = 0
				is_vassal = yes
				NOT = { liberty_desire = 50 }
				NOT = { overlord = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_e } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3 #simping for Irrliam
				F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_e }
				alliance_with = F37
			}
			modifier = { 
				factor = 2
				F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_e }
				has_opinion = { who = F37 value = 100 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0 #Elizna trolling
				F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_a }
				tag = U05 
			}
		}
			
		if = { limit = { F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_e } } #Increasing unity if picking the same option as Irrliam
			custom_tooltip = nsc_irrliam_option_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				if = { limit = { is_chosen_country = yes } #Elf choices count more
					REB = { change_variable = { which = nscIrrliamChoicesVar value = 2 } }
				}
				else = {
					REB = { change_variable = { which = nscIrrliamChoicesVar value = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { limit = { is_chosen_country = yes } #Elf choices count more
				REB = { change_variable = { which = nscChoiceEVar value = 2 } }
			}
			else = {
				REB = { change_variable = { which = nscChoiceEVar value = 1 } }
			}
			set_country_flag = nsc_choice_e
		}
		
		if = { limit = { NOT = { isolationism = 1 } } #moving toward an outcome raising the chosen's role if level < 1
			custom_tooltip = nsc_chosen_role_up_tt
			add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_death_of_taelarios value = 1 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_differing_opinion duration = 3650 }
		}
		else_if = { limit = { isolationism = 2 } #moving toward an outcome lowering the chosen's role if level > 1
			if = { limit = { isolationism = 3 }
				custom_tooltip = nsc_much_chosen_role_down_tt
				add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_death_of_taelarios value = -2 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_big_differing_opinion duration = 3650 }
			}
			else = {
				custom_tooltip = nsc_chosen_role_down_tt
				add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_death_of_taelarios value = -1 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_differing_opinion duration = 3650 }
			}
		}
		else = { #bonus for picking the option corresponding to your chosen's role level
			add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_congruent_opinion duration = 3650 }
		}
	}
	
	#unquestionable rulers
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.128.f
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = { factor = 0.1 isolationism = 1 }
			modifier = { #loyal vassals have to pick the same option as their overlords
				factor = 0
				is_vassal = yes
				NOT = { liberty_desire = 50 }
				NOT = { overlord = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_f } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3 #simping for Irrliam
				F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_f }
				alliance_with = F37
			}
			modifier = { 
				factor = 2
				F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_f }
				has_opinion = { who = F37 value = 100 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0 #Elizna trolling
				F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_a }
				tag = U05 
			}
		}
		
		if = { limit = { F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_f } } #Increasing unity if picking the same option as Irrliam
			custom_tooltip = nsc_irrliam_option_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				if = { limit = { is_chosen_country = yes } #Elf choices count more
					REB = { change_variable = { which = nscIrrliamChoicesVar value = 2 } }
				}
				else = {
					REB = { change_variable = { which = nscIrrliamChoicesVar value = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {	
			if = { limit = { is_chosen_country = yes } #Elf choices count more
				REB = { change_variable = { which = nscChoiceFVar value = 2 } }
			}
			else = {
				REB = { change_variable = { which = nscChoiceFVar value = 1 } }
			}
			set_country_flag = nsc_choice_f
		}
		
		if = { limit = { isolationism = 1 } #moving toward an outcome lowering the chosen's role if level > 0
			if = { limit = { isolationism = 2 }	
				custom_tooltip = nsc_much_chosen_role_down_tt
				add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_death_of_taelarios value = -2 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_big_differing_opinion duration = 3650 }
			}
			else = {
				custom_tooltip = nsc_chosen_role_down_tt
				add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_death_of_taelarios value = -1 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_differing_opinion duration = 3650 }
			}
		}
		else = { #bonus for picking the option corresponding to your chosen's role level
			add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_congruent_opinion duration = 3650 }
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { limit = { tag = F37 }	#Irrliam agreeing with itself
				REB = { change_variable = { which = nscIrrliamChoicesVar value = 2 } }
			}
			if = { limit = { is_chosen_country = yes }
				REB = { change_variable = { which = nscTotalChoicesVar value = 2 } }
			}
			else = {
				REB = { change_variable = { which = nscTotalChoicesVar value = 1 } }
			}
		}
	}
}

#Results
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.129
	title = new_sun_cult.129.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.129.d
	picture = REFORM_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			REB = {
				if = { limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = nsc_ratio_effect_applied } }
					set_country_flag = nsc_ratio_effect_applied
					nsc_get_choices_ratio_effect = yes
					nsc_unity_results = yes
				}
			}
			#triggering next debate
			if = { limit = { tag = F37 } 								#First Irrliam votes
				country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.130 days = 30 }
			}
			else_if = { limit = { is_vassal = no }						#Then independent countries
				country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.130 days = 180 }
			}
			else = {													#Then vassals
				country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.130 days = 330 }
			}
			country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.131 days = 480 }		#Results
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.129.a
		if = { limit = { REB = { check_variable = { which = nscIrrliamChoicesVar value = 66 } } }
			custom_tooltip = nsc_big_increase_unity_irrliam_tt
		}
		else_if = { limit = { REB = { check_variable = { which = nscIrrliamChoicesVar value = 33 } } }
			custom_tooltip = nsc_small_increase_unity_irrliam_tt
		}
		if = { 
			limit = {
				REB = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = { which = nscChoiceAVar value = 66 }
						check_variable = { which = nscChoiceBVar value = 66 }
						check_variable = { which = nscChoiceCVar value = 66 }
						check_variable = { which = nscChoiceEVar value = 66 }
						check_variable = { which = nscChoiceFVar value = 66 }
					}
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = nsc_big_increase_unity_same_tt
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = {
				REB = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = { which = nscChoiceAVar value = 33 }
						check_variable = { which = nscChoiceBVar value = 33 }
						check_variable = { which = nscChoiceCVar value = 33 }
						check_variable = { which = nscChoiceEVar value = 33 }
						check_variable = { which = nscChoiceFVar value = 33 }
					}
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = nsc_small_increase_unity_same_tt
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = nsc_stagnating_unity_tt
		}
		clr_country_flag = nsc_choice_a
		clr_country_flag = nsc_choice_b
		clr_country_flag = nsc_choice_c
		clr_country_flag = nsc_choice_e
		clr_country_flag = nsc_choice_f
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.130
	title = new_sun_cult.130.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.130.d
	picture = LIBERUM_VETO_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			REB = {
				if = { limit = { has_country_flag = nsc_ratio_effect_applied }
					nsc_init_choice_variables_effect = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	#Top positions should be elves
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.130.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = { #loyal vassals have to pick the same option as their overlords
				factor = 0
				is_vassal = yes
				NOT = { liberty_desire = 50 }
				NOT = { overlord = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_a } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3 #simping for Irrliam
				F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_a }
				alliance_with = F37
			}
			modifier = { 
				factor = 2
				F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_a }
				has_opinion = { who = F37 value = 100 }
			}
			modifier = { 
				factor = 0.5
				F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_a }
				is_rival = F37
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0 #Elizna trolling
				F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_a }
				tag = U05 
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0 #Humans not too happy about giving elves even more power
				OR = {
					is_vassal = no
					liberty_desire = 50
				}
				is_chosen_country = no
			}
		}
			
		if = { limit = { F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_a } } #Increasing unity if picking the same option as Irrliam
			custom_tooltip = nsc_irrliam_option_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				if = { limit = { is_chosen_country = yes } #Elf choices count more
					REB = { change_variable = { which = nscIrrliamChoicesVar value = 2 } }
				}
				else = {
					REB = { change_variable = { which = nscIrrliamChoicesVar value = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {	
			if = { limit = { is_chosen_country = yes } #Elf choices count more
				REB = { change_variable = { which = nscChoiceAVar value = 2 } }
			}
			else = {
				REB = { change_variable = { which = nscChoiceAVar value = 1 } }
			}
			set_country_flag = nsc_choice_a
		}
		
		custom_tooltip = nsc_chosen_role_up_tt
		add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_death_of_taelarios value = 1 }
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_elven_clergy_support duration = 9125 }
	}
	
	#no need to change anything
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.130.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = { #loyal vassals have to pick the same option as their overlords
				factor = 0
				is_vassal = yes
				NOT = { liberty_desire = 50 }
				NOT = { overlord = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_b } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3 #simping for Irrliam
				F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_b }
				alliance_with = F37
			}
			modifier = { 
				factor = 2
				F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_b }
				has_opinion = { who = F37 value = 100 }
			}
			modifier = { 
				factor = 0.5
				F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_b }
				is_rival = F37
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0 #Elizna trolling
				F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_b }
				tag = U05 
			}
		}
			
		if = { limit = { F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_b } } #Increasing unity if picking the same option as Irrliam
			custom_tooltip = nsc_irrliam_option_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				if = { limit = { is_chosen_country = yes } #Elf choices count more
					REB = { change_variable = { which = nscIrrliamChoicesVar value = 2 } }
				}
				else = {
					REB = { change_variable = { which = nscIrrliamChoicesVar value = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {	
			if = { limit = { is_chosen_country = yes } #Elf choices count more
				REB = { change_variable = { which = nscChoiceBVar value = 2 } }
			}
			else = {
				REB = { change_variable = { which = nscChoiceBVar value = 1 } }
			}
			set_country_flag = nsc_choice_b
		}
		
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_human_clergy_support duration = 9125 }
	}
	
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {

			}
			if = { limit = { is_chosen_country = yes }
				REB = { change_variable = { which = nscTotalChoicesVar value = 2 } }
			}
			else = {
				REB = { change_variable = { which = nscTotalChoicesVar value = 1 } }
			}
		}
	}
}

			set_country_flag = nsc_choice_b
		}
		
		custom_tooltip = nsc_chosen_role_up_tt
		add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_death_of_taelarios value = 1 }
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_converting_heretics duration = 3650 }
	}
	
	#They pose no threat to us
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.132.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = { #loyal vassals have to pick the same option as their overlords
				factor = 0
				is_vassal = yes
				NOT = { liberty_desire = 50 }
				NOT = { overlord = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_c } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3 #simping for Irrliam
				F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_c }
				alliance_with = F37
			}
			modifier = { 
				factor = 2
				F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_c }
				has_opinion = { who = F37 value = 100 }
			}
			modifier = { 
				factor = 0.5
				F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_c }
				is_rival = F37
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0 #Elizna trolling
				F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_c }
				tag = U05 
			}
		}
			
		if = { limit = { F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_c } } #Increasing unity if picking the same option as Irrliam
			custom_tooltip = nsc_irrliam_option_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				if = { limit = { is_chosen_country = yes } #Elf choices count more
					REB = { change_variable = { which = nscIrrliamChoicesVar value = 2 } }
				}
				else = {
					REB = { change_variable = { which = nscIrrliamChoicesVar value = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {	
			if = { limit = { is_chosen_country = yes } #Elf choices count more
				REB = { change_variable = { which = nscChoiceCVar value = 2 } }
			}
			else = {
				REB = { change_variable = { which = nscChoiceCVar value = 1 } }
			}
			set_country_flag = nsc_choice_c
		}
		
		custom_tooltip = nsc_chosen_role_down_tt
		add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_death_of_taelarios value = -1 }
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_ignoring_heretics duration = 3650 }
	}
	
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { limit = { tag = F37 }	#Irrliam agreeing with itself
				REB = { change_variable = { which = nscIrrliamChoicesVar value = 2 } }
			}
			if = { limit = { is_chosen_country = yes }
				REB = { change_variable = { which = nscTotalChoicesVar value = 2 } }
			}
			else = {
				REB = { change_variable = { which = nscTotalChoicesVar value = 1 } }
			}
		}
	}
}

#Results
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.133
	title = new_sun_cult.133.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.133.d
	picture = REFORM_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			REB = {
				if = { limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = nsc_ratio_effect_applied } }
					set_country_flag = nsc_ratio_effect_applied
					nsc_get_choices_ratio_effect = yes
					nsc_unity_results = yes
				}
			}
			#triggering next debate
			if = { limit = { tag = F37 } 								#First Irrliam votes
				country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.134 days = 30 }
			}
			else_if = { limit = { is_vassal = no }						#Then independent countries
				country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.134 days = 180 }
			}
			else = {													#Then vassals
				country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.134 days = 330 }
			}
			country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.135 days = 480 }		#Results
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.133.a
		if = { limit = { REB = { check_variable = { which = nscIrrliamChoicesVar value = 66 } } }
			custom_tooltip = nsc_big_increase_unity_irrliam_tt
		}
		else_if = { limit = { REB = { check_variable = { which = nscIrrliamChoicesVar value = 33 } } }
			custom_tooltip = nsc_small_increase_unity_irrliam_tt
		}
		if = { 
			limit = {
				REB = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = { which = nscChoiceAVar value = 66 }
						check_variable = { which = nscChoiceBVar value = 66 }
						check_variable = { which = nscChoiceCVar value = 66 }
					}
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = nsc_big_increase_unity_same_tt
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = {
				REB = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = { which = nscChoiceAVar value = 33 }
						check_variable = { which = nscChoiceBVar value = 33 }
						check_variable = { which = nscChoiceCVar value = 33 }
					}
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = nsc_small_increase_unity_same_tt
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = nsc_stagnating_unity_tt
		}
		clr_country_flag = nsc_choice_a
		clr_country_flag = nsc_choice_b
		clr_country_flag = nsc_choice_c
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.136
	title = new_sun_cult.136.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.136.d
	picture = DIPLOMACY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {

				if = { limit = { has_country_flag = nsc_ratio_effect_applied }
					nsc_init_choice_variables_effect = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	#The council will take them
	option = {

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = { #loyal vassals have to pick the same option as their overlords

			else = {
				REB = { change_variable = { which = nscChoiceBVar value = 1 } }
			}
			set_country_flag = nsc_choice_b
		}
		
		add_prestige = 5
	}
	
	#Disband them
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.136.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = { #loyal vassals have to pick the same option as their overlords
				factor = 0
				is_vassal = yes
				NOT = { liberty_desire = 50 }
				NOT = { overlord = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_c } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3 #simping for Irrliam
				F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_c }
				alliance_with = F37
			}
			modifier = { 
				factor = 2
				F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_c }
				has_opinion = { who = F37 value = 100 }
			}
			modifier = { 
				factor = 0.5
				F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_c }
				is_rival = F37
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0 #Elizna trolling

			hidden_effect = {
