		}
		hidden_effect = {	
			if = { limit = { is_chosen_country = yes } #Elf choices count more
				REB = { change_variable = { which = nscChoiceCVar value = 2 } }
			}
			else = {
				REB = { change_variable = { which = nscChoiceCVar value = 1 } }
			}
			set_country_flag = nsc_choice_c
		}
		
		custom_tooltip = nsc_chosen_role_down_tt
		add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_death_of_taelarios value = -1 }
	}
	
	#Irrliam should keep them
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.136.a
		trigger = { exists = F37 }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = { #loyal vassals have to pick the same option as their overlords
				factor = 0
				is_vassal = yes
				NOT = { liberty_desire = 50 }
				NOT = { overlord = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_a } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3 #simping for Irrliam
				F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_a }
				alliance_with = F37
			}
			modifier = { 
				factor = 2
				F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_a }
				has_opinion = { who = F37 value = 100 }
			}
			modifier = { 
				factor = 0.5
				F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_a }
				is_rival = F37
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0 #Elizna trolling
				F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_a }
				tag = U05 
			}
		}
			
		if = { limit = { F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_a } } #Increasing unity if picking the same option as Irrliam
			custom_tooltip = nsc_irrliam_option_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				if = { limit = { is_chosen_country = yes } #Elf choices count more
					REB = { change_variable = { which = nscIrrliamChoicesVar value = 2 } }
				}
				else = {
					REB = { change_variable = { which = nscIrrliamChoicesVar value = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {	
			if = { limit = { is_chosen_country = yes } #Elf choices count more
				REB = { change_variable = { which = nscChoiceAVar value = 2 } }
			}
			else = {
				REB = { change_variable = { which = nscChoiceAVar value = 1 } }
			}
			set_country_flag = nsc_choice_a
		}
		
		reverse_add_opinion = { who = F37 modifier = nsc_supporting_irrliam }
	}
	
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { limit = { tag = F37 }	#Irrliam agreeing with itself
				REB = { change_variable = { which = nscIrrliamChoicesVar value = 2 } }
			}
			if = { limit = { is_chosen_country = yes }
				REB = { change_variable = { which = nscTotalChoicesVar value = 2 } }
			}
			else = {
				REB = { change_variable = { which = nscTotalChoicesVar value = 1 } }
			}
		}
	}
}

			else = {													#Then vassals
				country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.138 days = 330 }
			}
			country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.139 days = 480 }		#Results
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.137.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				REB = {
					check_variable = { which = nscChoiceAVar which = nscChoiceBVar }
					check_variable = { which = nscChoiceAVar which = nscChoiceCVar }
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = nsc_irrliam_keeps_the_order_tt
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = {
				REB = {
					check_variable = { which = nscChoiceBVar which = nscChoiceAVar }
					check_variable = { which = nscChoiceBVar which = nscChoiceCVar }
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = nsc_everyone_get_the_order_tt
			set_country_flag = order_of_the_zenith
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = nsc_disband_the_order_tt
			if = { limit = { tag = F37 }
				clr_country_flag = order_of_the_zenith
			}
		}
		if = { limit = { REB = { check_variable = { which = nscIrrliamChoicesVar value = 66 } } }
			custom_tooltip = nsc_big_increase_unity_irrliam_tt
		}
		else_if = { limit = { REB = { check_variable = { which = nscIrrliamChoicesVar value = 33 } } }
			custom_tooltip = nsc_small_increase_unity_irrliam_tt
		}
		if = { 
			limit = {
				REB = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = { which = nscChoiceAVar value = 66 }
						check_variable = { which = nscChoiceBVar value = 66 }
						check_variable = { which = nscChoiceCVar value = 66 }
					}
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = nsc_big_increase_unity_same_tt
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = {
				REB = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = { which = nscChoiceAVar value = 50 }
						check_variable = { which = nscChoiceBVar value = 50 }
						check_variable = { which = nscChoiceCVar value = 50 }
					}
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = nsc_small_increase_unity_same_tt
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = nsc_stagnating_unity_tt
		}
		clr_country_flag = nsc_choice_a
		clr_country_flag = nsc_choice_b
		clr_country_flag = nsc_choice_c
	}
}

#Local Festivals
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.138
	title = new_sun_cult.138.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.138.d
	picture = CITY_DEVELOPMENT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			REB = {
				if = { limit = { has_country_flag = nsc_ratio_effect_applied }
					nsc_init_choice_variables_effect = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	#Fund them
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.138.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = { #loyal vassals have to pick the same option as their overlords
				factor = 0
				is_vassal = yes
				NOT = { liberty_desire = 50 }
				NOT = { overlord = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_a } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3 #simping for Irrliam
				F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_a }
				alliance_with = F37
			}
			modifier = { 
				factor = 2
				F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_a }
				has_opinion = { who = F37 value = 100 }
			}
			modifier = { 
				factor = 0.5
				F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_a }
				is_rival = F37
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0 #Elizna trolling
				F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_a }
				tag = U05 
			}
		}
			
		if = { limit = { F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_a } } #Increasing unity if picking the same option as Irrliam
			custom_tooltip = nsc_irrliam_option_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				if = { limit = { is_chosen_country = yes } #Elf choices count more
					REB = { change_variable = { which = nscIrrliamChoicesVar value = 2 } }
				}
				else = {
					REB = { change_variable = { which = nscIrrliamChoicesVar value = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {	
			if = { limit = { is_chosen_country = yes } #Elf choices count more
				REB = { change_variable = { which = nscChoiceAVar value = 2 } }
			}
			else = {
				REB = { change_variable = { which = nscChoiceAVar value = 1 } }
			}
			set_country_flag = nsc_choice_a
		}
		
		custom_tooltip = nsc_chosen_role_up_tt
		add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_death_of_taelarios value = 1 }
		set_country_flag = nsc_sponsored_festivals_flag
		set_estate_privilege = estate_church_sponsored_festivals
	}
	
	#Just equip them
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.138.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = { #loyal vassals have to pick the same option as their overlords
				factor = 0
				is_vassal = yes
				NOT = { liberty_desire = 50 }
				NOT = { overlord = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_b } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3 #simping for Irrliam
				F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_b }
				alliance_with = F37
			}
			modifier = { 
				factor = 2
				F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_b }
				has_opinion = { who = F37 value = 100 }
			}
			modifier = { 
				factor = 0.5
				F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_b }
				is_rival = F37
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0 #Elizna trolling
				F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_b }
				tag = U05 
			}
		}
			
		if = { limit = { F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_b } } #Increasing unity if picking the same option as Irrliam
			custom_tooltip = nsc_irrliam_option_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				if = { limit = { is_chosen_country = yes } #Elf choices count more
					REB = { change_variable = { which = nscIrrliamChoicesVar value = 2 } }
				}
				else = {
					REB = { change_variable = { which = nscIrrliamChoicesVar value = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {	
			if = { limit = { is_chosen_country = yes } #Elf choices count more
				REB = { change_variable = { which = nscChoiceBVar value = 2 } }
			}
			else = {
				REB = { change_variable = { which = nscChoiceBVar value = 1 } }
			}
			set_country_flag = nsc_choice_b
		}
		
		add_treasury = -50
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_equipped_festivals duration = 3650 }
	}
	
	#Tax them
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.138.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = { #loyal vassals have to pick the same option as their overlords
				factor = 0
				is_vassal = yes
				NOT = { liberty_desire = 50 }
				NOT = { overlord = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_c } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3 #simping for Irrliam
				F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_c }
				alliance_with = F37
			}
			modifier = { 
				factor = 2
				F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_c }
				has_opinion = { who = F37 value = 100 }
			}
			modifier = { 
				factor = 0.5
				F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_c }
				is_rival = F37
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0 #Elizna trolling
				F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_c }
				tag = U05 
			}
		}
			
		if = { limit = { F37 = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_c } } #Increasing unity if picking the same option as Irrliam
			custom_tooltip = nsc_irrliam_option_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				if = { limit = { is_chosen_country = yes } #Elf choices count more
					REB = { change_variable = { which = nscIrrliamChoicesVar value = 2 } }
				}
				else = {
					REB = { change_variable = { which = nscIrrliamChoicesVar value = 1 } }
				}

			}
			else = {

			}
			set_country_flag = nsc_choice_c

		custom_tooltip = nsc_chosen_role_down_tt
		add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_death_of_taelarios value = -1 }
		set_country_flag = nsc_church_tax_on_festivals
		set_estate_privilege = estate_church_tax_on_local_festivals
	}
	
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { limit = { tag = F37 }	#Irrliam agreeing with itself
				REB = { change_variable = { which = nscIrrliamChoicesVar value = 2 } }
			}
			if = { limit = { is_chosen_country = yes }
				REB = { change_variable = { which = nscTotalChoicesVar value = 2 } }
			}
			else = {
				REB = { change_variable = { which = nscTotalChoicesVar value = 1 } }
			}
		}
	}
}

#Results
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.139
	title = new_sun_cult.139.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.139.d
	picture = REFORM_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			REB = {
				if = { limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = nsc_ratio_effect_applied } }
					set_country_flag = nsc_ratio_effect_applied
					nsc_get_choices_ratio_effect = yes
					nsc_unity_results = yes
				}
			}
			#triggering next debate
			if = { limit = { tag = F37 } 								#First Irrliam votes
				country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.140 days = 30 }
			}
			else_if = { limit = { is_vassal = no }						#Then independent countries
				country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.140 days = 180 }
			}
			else = {													#Then vassals
				country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.140 days = 330 }
			}
			country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.141 days = 480 }		#Results
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.139.a
		if = { limit = { REB = { check_variable = { which = nscIrrliamChoicesVar value = 66 } } }
			custom_tooltip = nsc_big_increase_unity_irrliam_tt
		}
		else_if = { limit = { REB = { check_variable = { which = nscIrrliamChoicesVar value = 33 } } }
			custom_tooltip = nsc_small_increase_unity_irrliam_tt
		}
		if = { 
			limit = {
				REB = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = { which = nscChoiceAVar value = 66 }
						check_variable = { which = nscChoiceBVar value = 66 }
						check_variable = { which = nscChoiceCVar value = 66 }
					}
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = nsc_big_increase_unity_same_tt
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = {
				REB = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = { which = nscChoiceAVar value = 33 }
						check_variable = { which = nscChoiceBVar value = 33 }
						check_variable = { which = nscChoiceCVar value = 33 }
					}
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = nsc_small_increase_unity_same_tt
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = nsc_stagnating_unity_tt
		}
		clr_country_flag = nsc_choice_a
		clr_country_flag = nsc_choice_b
		clr_country_flag = nsc_choice_c
	}
}

#Results
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.141
	title = new_sun_cult.141.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.141.d
	picture = REFORM_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			REB = {
				if = { limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = nsc_ratio_effect_applied } }
					set_country_flag = nsc_ratio_effect_applied
					nsc_get_choices_ratio_effect = yes
					nsc_unity_results = yes
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.142 days = 150 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.141.a
		if = { limit = { REB = { check_variable = { which = nscIrrliamChoicesVar value = 66 } } }
			custom_tooltip = nsc_big_increase_unity_irrliam_tt
		}
		else_if = { limit = { REB = { check_variable = { which = nscIrrliamChoicesVar value = 33 } } }
			custom_tooltip = nsc_small_increase_unity_irrliam_tt
		}
		if = { 
			limit = {
				REB = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = { which = nscChoiceAVar value = 66 }
						check_variable = { which = nscChoiceBVar value = 66 }
						check_variable = { which = nscChoiceCVar value = 66 }
					}
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = nsc_big_increase_unity_same_tt
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = {
				REB = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = { which = nscChoiceAVar value = 33 }
						check_variable = { which = nscChoiceBVar value = 33 }
						check_variable = { which = nscChoiceCVar value = 33 }
					}
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = nsc_small_increase_unity_same_tt
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = nsc_stagnating_unity_tt
		}
		if = { limit = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_a }
			every_known_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_a }
				add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = nsc_similar_views }
			}
			every_known_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_b }
				add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = nsc_different_views }
			}
			every_known_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_c }
				add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = nsc_very_different_views }
			}
		}
		if = { limit = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_b }
			every_known_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_a }
				add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = nsc_different_views }
			}
			every_known_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_b }
				add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = nsc_similar_views }
			}
			every_known_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_c }
				add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = nsc_very_different_views }
			}
		}
		if = { limit = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_c }
			every_known_country = {
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = nsc_choice_a
						has_country_flag = nsc_choice_b
					}
				}
				add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = nsc_very_different_views }
			}
			every_known_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = nsc_choice_c }
				add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = nsc_very_similar_views }
			}
		}
	}
}

#Council Ends
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.142
	title = new_sun_cult.142.t
	desc = { trigger = { REB = { check_variable = { which = nscUnityVar value = 600 } } } desc = new_sun_cult.142.da } #High unity
	desc = {																			 								#Medium unity
		trigger = {
			REB = {
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = nscUnityVar value = 600 } }
				check_variable = { which = nscUnityVar value = 300 }
			}
		}
		desc = new_sun_cult.142.db
	}
	desc = { trigger = { REB = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = nscUnityVar value = 300 } } } } desc = new_sun_cult.142.dc } #Low unity
	picture = { trigger = { REB = { check_variable = { which = nscUnityVar value = 600 } } } picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture }
	picture = {
		trigger = {
			REB = {
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = nscUnityVar value = 600 } }
				check_variable = { which = nscUnityVar value = 300 }
			}
		}
		picture = CULTURE_eventPicture
	}
	picture = { trigger = { REB = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = nscUnityVar value = 300 } } } } picture = BAD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture }
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			REB = {
				if = { limit = { has_country_flag = nsc_ratio_effect_applied }
					nsc_init_choice_variables_effect = yes
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = had_nsc_incident_flag
			clr_country_flag = nsc_choice_a
			clr_country_flag = nsc_choice_b
			clr_country_flag = nsc_choice_c
		}
	}
	
	#High unity
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.142.a
		trigger = { REB = { check_variable = { which = nscUnityVar value = 600 } } }
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_divided_cult
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_big_council
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_medium_council
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_small_council
		if = { limit = { tag = F37 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_unified_cult duration = 18250 }
		}
	}
	
	#Medium unity
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.142.b
		trigger = {
			REB = {
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = nscUnityVar value = 600 } }
				check_variable = { which = nscUnityVar value = 300 }
			}			
		}
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_divided_cult
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_big_council
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_medium_council
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_small_council
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_restructuring_cult duration = 9125 }
	}
	
	#Low unity
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.142.c
		trigger = { REB = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = nscUnityVar value = 300 } } } }
		hidden_effect = { remove_country_modifier = nsc_divided_cult }
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_divided_cult duration = 9125 }
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_big_council
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_medium_council
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_small_council
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_autonomous_clergy duration = 9125 }
	}
	
	after = {
		country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.143 }
	}
}

#Personal stances results
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.143
	title = new_sun_cult.143.t
	desc = { trigger = { incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_death_of_taelarios value = 2 } } desc = new_sun_cult.143.da }
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_death_of_taelarios value = 2 } }
			incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_death_of_taelarios value = -2 }
		}
		desc = new_sun_cult.143.db
	}
	desc = { trigger = { NOT = { incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_death_of_taelarios value = -2 } } } desc = new_sun_cult.143.dc }
	picture = { trigger = { incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_death_of_taelarios value = 2 } } picture = HAJJ_eventPicture }
	picture = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_death_of_taelarios value = 2 } }
			incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_death_of_taelarios value = -2 }
		}
		picture = PRAYING_eventPicture
	}
	picture = { trigger = { NOT = { incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_death_of_taelarios value = -2 } } } picture = CULTURE_eventPicture }
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Zealous stance
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.143.a
		trigger = { incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_death_of_taelarios value = 2 } }				#max possible -6
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_zealous_stance duration = 9125 }
		increase_nsc_isolation_level = yes
		end_incident = incident_death_of_taelarios
	}
	
	#Moderate stance
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.143.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_death_of_taelarios value = 2 } }
			incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_death_of_taelarios value = -2 }
		}
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_moderate_stance duration = 9125 }
		end_incident = incident_death_of_taelarios
	}
	
	#Tolerance stance
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.143.c
		trigger = { NOT = { incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_death_of_taelarios value = -2 } } }		#min possible +7
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_tolerant_stance duration = 9125 }
		decrease_nsc_isolation_level = yes
		end_incident = incident_death_of_taelarios
	}
	
	after = {
		clr_country_flag = active_nsc_incident_flag
	}
}

			modifier = { 	factor = 5 ruler_has_personality = careful_personality }
			modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { years_of_income = 0.2 } }
		}
		custom_tooltip = nsc_chosen_role_down_tt

				55 = { country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.151 days = 730 } } #expedition success

		}
	}
	
	#Fund them and give them some ships

			random_list = {
				55 = { country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.150 days = 730 } } #expedition great success
				35 = { country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.151 days = 730 } } #expedition success
				10 = { country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.152 days = 730 } } #expedition success
			}
		}
	}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 33
			modifier = { factor = 10 ruler_has_personality = careful_personality }

#Disgruntled sun elf officers
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.153
	title = new_sun_cult.153.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.153.d
	picture = MILITARY_CAMP_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Let them go
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.153.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 33
			modifier = { factor = 100 personality = ai_colonialist }
			modifier = { factor = 10 ruler_has_personality = expansionist_personality }
			modifier = { factor = 5 ruler_has_personality = naive_personality }
		}
		custom_tooltip = nsc_chosen_role_down_tt
		add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_call_of_aelantir value = 1 }
		add_manpower = -5
		add_army_tradition = -5
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_officers_left duration = 3650 }
	}
	
	#Force them to stay
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.153.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 33
			modifier = { factor = 10 ruler_has_personality = strict_personality }
		}
		custom_tooltip = nsc_chosen_role_up_tt
		add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_call_of_aelantir value = -1 }
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_disgruntled_officers duration = 3650 }
		if = { limit = { num_of_owned_provinces_with = { culture = sun_elf value = 1 } }
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = { culture = sun_elf }
				spawn_rebels = { type = noble_rebels size = 1 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			random_owned_province = {
				spawn_rebels = { type = noble_rebels size = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	#Reform the army to convince them to stay
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.153.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 33
			modifier = { factor = 5 ruler_has_personality = tactical_genius_personality }
			modifier = { factor = 5 ruler_has_personality = martial_educator_personality }
		}
		custom_tooltip = nsc_much_chosen_role_up_tt
		add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_call_of_aelantir value = -2 }
		add_mil_power = -100
		add_army_tradition = 5
		
	}
	
	#Have your ruler convince them to stay
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.153.e
		highlight = yes
		trigger = {

			}

		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_bullshited_officers duration = 3650 }
	}

	}

			}

			modifier = { factor = 10 ruler_has_personality = expansionist_personality }

	}

					trade_goods = copper
				}
			}

				}
			}

#Incident Outcome
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.158
	title = new_sun_cult.158.t
	desc = { trigger = { incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_call_of_aelantir value = 4 } } desc = new_sun_cult.158.da }
	desc = {
		trigger = {
				NOT = { incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_call_of_aelantir value = 4 } }
				incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_call_of_aelantir value = -2 }
		}
		desc = new_sun_cult.158.db
	}
	desc = { trigger = { NOT = { incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_call_of_aelantir value = -2 } } } desc = new_sun_cult.158.dc }
	picture = { trigger = { incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_call_of_aelantir value = 4 } } picture = PILGRIMAGE_eventPicture }
	picture = {
		trigger = {
				NOT = { incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_call_of_aelantir value = 4 } }
				incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_call_of_aelantir value = -2 }
		}
		picture = COLONIZATION_eventPicture
	}
	picture = { trigger = { NOT = { incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_call_of_aelantir value = -2 } } } picture = FARMING_eventPicture }
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#High enthusiasm
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.158.a
		trigger = { incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_call_of_aelantir value = 4 } } 				#max possible -10
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_high_aelantir_enthusiasm duration = 18250 }
		decrease_nsc_isolation_level = yes
		end_incident = incident_call_of_aelantir
	}
	
	#Mid enthusiasm
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.158.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_call_of_aelantir value = 4 } }
			incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_call_of_aelantir value = -2 }
		}
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_moderate_aelantir_enthusiasm duration = 18250 }
		end_incident = incident_call_of_aelantir
	}
	
	#Low enthusiasm
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.158.c
		trigger = { NOT = { incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_call_of_aelantir value = -2 } } }	#min possible +8
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_low_aelantir_enthusiasm duration = 18250 }
		increase_nsc_isolation_level = yes
		end_incident = incident_call_of_aelantir
	}
	
	after = {
		clr_country_flag = active_nsc_incident_flag
		set_country_flag = had_nsc_incident_flag
	}
}

#----------# Summit of Samartal #----------#

#Tension events spinning wheel
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.160
	title = new_sun_cult.160.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.160.d
	picture = FARMING_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_global_flag = nsc_summit_of_sammartal_started }
		is_year = 1455
		religion = bulwari_sun_cult
		has_dlc = "Mandate of Heaven"
		is_incident_potential = incident_summit_of_samartal
		any_known_country = {
			religion = bulwari_sun_cult
			is_incident_potential = incident_summit_of_samartal
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_known_country = {
			limit = {
				religion = bulwari_sun_cult
				NOT = { capital_scope = { continent = south_america } }
				NOT = { capital_scope = { continent = north_america } }
			}
			save_event_target_as = nsc_target_country
		}
		random_known_country = {
			limit = {
				religion = bulwari_sun_cult
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
						NOT = { liberty_desire = 50 }
					}
				}
				NOT = { capital_scope = { continent = south_america } }
				NOT = { capital_scope = { continent = north_america } }
			}
			save_event_target_as = nsc_target_country
		}
		random_known_country = {
			limit = {
				religion = bulwari_sun_cult
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
						NOT = { liberty_desire = 50 }
					}
				}
				NOT = { capital_scope = { continent = south_america } }
				NOT = { capital_scope = { continent = north_america } }
				NOT = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = nsc_suspicious_behaviour_big } }
			}
			save_event_target_as = nsc_target_country
		}
		random_known_country = {
			limit = {
				religion = bulwari_sun_cult
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
						NOT = { liberty_desire = 50 }
					}
				}
				NOT = { capital_scope = { continent = south_america } }
				NOT = { capital_scope = { continent = north_america } }
				NOT = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = nsc_suspicious_behaviour_big } }
				NOT = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = nsc_suspicious_behaviour } }
			}
			save_event_target_as = nsc_target_country
		}
		random_known_country = {
			limit = {
				religion = bulwari_sun_cult
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
						NOT = { liberty_desire = 50 }
					}
				}
				NOT = { capital_scope = { continent = south_america } }
				NOT = { capital_scope = { continent = north_america } }
				NOT = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = nsc_suspicious_behaviour_big } }
				NOT = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = nsc_suspicious_behaviour } }
				NOT = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
			}
			save_event_target_as = nsc_target_country
		}
		random_known_country = {
			limit = {
				religion = bulwari_sun_cult
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
						NOT = { liberty_desire = 50 }
					}
				}
				NOT = { capital_scope = { continent = south_america } }
				NOT = { capital_scope = { continent = north_america } }
				NOT = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = nsc_suspicious_behaviour_big } }
				NOT = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = nsc_suspicious_behaviour } }
				alliance_with = ROOT
			}
			save_event_target_as = nsc_target_country
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.160.a
		random_list = {
			10 = {
				trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = nsc_assassination_attempt } has_regency = no }
				country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.161 } #+3 tension
			}
			10 = {
				trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = nsc_kidnapping } has_heir = yes }
				country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.163 } #+3 tension
			}
			10 = {
				modifier = { factor = 0.02 has_country_flag = nsc_arson }
				random_owned_province = { province_event = { id = new_sun_cult.166 } } #+1 tension
			}
			10 = {
				modifier = { factor = 0.02 has_country_flag = nsc_caravan_raided }
				country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.167 } #+1 tension
			}
			10 = {
				modifier = { factor = 0.01 has_country_flag = nsc_instigated_revolts }
				random_owned_province = { province_event = { id = new_sun_cult.168 } } #+2 tension
			}
			100 = {
				trigger = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = nscNoTensionEvent value = 10 } } }
				modifier = { factor = 0.5 check_variable = { which = nscNoTensionEvent value = 9 } }
				modifier = { factor = 0.66 check_variable = { which = nscNoTensionEvent value = 8 } }
				modifier = { factor = 0.75 check_variable = { which = nscNoTensionEvent value = 7 } }
				modifier = { factor = 0.8 check_variable = { which = nscNoTensionEvent value = 6 } }
				modifier = { factor = 0.85 check_variable = { which = nscNoTensionEvent value = 5 } }
				modifier = { factor = 0.85 check_variable = { which = nscNoTensionEvent value = 4 } }
				modifier = { factor = 0.85 check_variable = { which = nscNoTensionEvent value = 3 } }
				modifier = { factor = 0.9 check_variable = { which = nscNoTensionEvent value = 2 } }
				modifier = { factor = 0.9 check_variable = { which = nscNoTensionEvent value = 1 } }
				modifier = { factor = 0.5 NOT = { calc_true_if = { all_known_country = { is_incident_potential = incident_summit_of_samartal } amount = 20 } } }
				modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { calc_true_if = { all_known_country = { is_incident_potential = incident_summit_of_samartal } amount = 11 } } }
				modifier = { factor = 0 is_year = 1480 }
				change_variable = { which = nscNoTensionEvent value = 1 }
			}
		}
		#on average, tension increase by 1 every time this event fires
	}
}

#Failed assassination attempt
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.161
	title = new_sun_cult.161.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.161.d
	picture = ASSASSINATION_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Hire the best surgeon
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.161.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				variable_arithmetic_trigger = {
					export_to_variable = { which = rulerAdmVar value = ADM }
					export_to_variable = { which = rulerDipVar value = DIP }
					export_to_variable = { which = rulerMilVar value = MIL }
					change_variable = { which = rulerAdmVar which = rulerDipVar }
					change_variable = { which = rulerAdmVar which = rulerMilVar }
					check_variable = { which = rulerAdmVar value = 9 }
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = nsc_assassination_attempt
		nsc_increase_tension_large_effect = yes
		add_treasury = -50
		if = { limit = { adm = 2 }
			change_adm = -2
			set_ruler_flag = nsc_adm_2
		}
		else_if = { limit = { adm = 1 }
			change_adm = -1
			set_ruler_flag = nsc_adm_1
		}
		if = { limit = { dip = 2 }
			change_dip = -2
			set_ruler_flag = nsc_dip_2
		}
		else_if = { limit = { dip = 1 }
			change_dip = -1
			set_ruler_flag = nsc_dip_1
		}
		if = { limit = { mil = 2 }
			change_mil = -2
			set_ruler_flag = nsc_mil_2
		}
		else_if = { limit = { mil = 1 }
			change_mil = -1
			set_ruler_flag = nsc_mil_1
		}
		add_ruler_modifier = { name = nsc_wounded_ruler duration = 270 }
		add_trust = { who = event_target:nsc_target_country value = -25 }
		add_opinion = { who = event_target:nsc_target_country modifier = nsc_suspicious_behaviour_big }
	}
	
	#Place his/her fate in the hands of Surael
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.161.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				variable_arithmetic_trigger = {
					export_to_variable = { which = rulerAdmVar value = ADM }
					export_to_variable = { which = rulerDipVar value = DIP }
					export_to_variable = { which = rulerMilVar value = MIL }
					change_variable = { which = rulerAdmVar which = rulerDipVar }
					change_variable = { which = rulerAdmVar which = rulerMilVar }
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = rulerAdmVar value = 9 } }
				}
			}
			modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { heir_age = 15 } }
			modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { stability = 0 } }
		}
		set_country_flag = nsc_assassination_attempt
		nsc_increase_tension_large_effect = yes
		if = { limit = { adm = 2 }
			change_adm = -2
			set_ruler_flag = nsc_adm_2
		}
		else_if = { limit = { adm = 1 }
			change_adm = -1
			set_ruler_flag = nsc_adm_1
		}
		if = { limit = { dip = 2 }
			change_dip = -2
			set_ruler_flag = nsc_dip_2
		}
		else_if = { limit = { dip = 1 }
			change_dip = -1
			set_ruler_flag = nsc_dip_1
		}
		if = { limit = { mil = 2 }
			change_mil = -2
			set_ruler_flag = nsc_mil_2
		}
		else_if = { limit = { mil = 1 }
			change_mil = -1
			set_ruler_flag = nsc_mil_1
		}
		add_ruler_modifier = { name = nsc_wounded_ruler duration = 270 }
		add_trust = { who = event_target:nsc_target_country value = -25 }
		add_opinion = { who = event_target:nsc_target_country modifier = nsc_suspicious_behaviour_big }
		custom_tooltip = nsc_ruler_may_die_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			random = { chance = 50 set_ruler_flag = nsc_ruler_will_die }
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.162 days = 269 }
		event_target:nsc_target_country = {
			set_country_flag = nsc_assassination_attempt_on_@ROOT
			country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.169 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

#Ruler's fate
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.162
	title = new_sun_cult.162.t
	desc = { trigger = { NOT = { has_ruler_flag = nsc_ruler_will_die } } desc = new_sun_cult.162.da }
	desc = { trigger = { has_ruler_flag = nsc_ruler_will_die } desc = new_sun_cult.162.db }
	picture = KING_SICK_IN_BED_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_ruler_modifier = nsc_wounded_ruler
	}
	
	#Ruler recovers
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.162.a
		trigger = { NOT = { has_ruler_flag = nsc_ruler_will_die } }
		if = { limit = { has_ruler_flag = nsc_adm_2 }
			change_adm = 2
		}
		if = { limit = { has_ruler_flag = nsc_adm_1 }
			change_adm = 1
		}
		if = { limit = { has_ruler_flag = nsc_dip_2 }
			change_dip = 2
		}
		if = { limit = { has_ruler_flag = nsc_dip_1 }
			change_dip = 1
		}
		if = { limit = { has_ruler_flag = nsc_mil_2 }
			change_mil = 2
		}
		if = { limit = { has_ruler_flag = nsc_mil_1 }
			change_mil = 1
		}
	}
	
	#Ruler dies
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.162.b
		trigger = { has_ruler_flag = nsc_ruler_will_die }
		kill_ruler = yes
	}
	
	after = {
		clr_ruler_flag = nsc_adm_2
		clr_ruler_flag = nsc_adm_1
		clr_ruler_flag = nsc_dip_2
		clr_ruler_flag = nsc_dip_1
		clr_ruler_flag = nsc_mil_2
		clr_ruler_flag = nsc_mil_1
	}
}

		name = new_sun_cult.164.a

			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				variable_arithmetic_trigger = {
					export_to_variable = { which = heirAdmVar value = heir_adm }
					export_to_variable = { which = heirDipVar value = heir_dip }
					export_to_variable = { which = heirMilVar value = heir_mil }
					change_variable = { which = heirAdmVar which = heirDipVar }
					change_variable = { which = heirAdmVar which = heirMilVar }
					check_variable = { which = heirAdmVar value = 9 }
				}
			}
			modifier = { factor = 0 num_of_loans = 5 }
		}
		add_treasury = -100
		country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.165 days = 180 }
	}
	
	#Don't pay
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.164.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1

					export_to_variable = { which = heirAdmVar value = heir_adm }
					export_to_variable = { which = heirDipVar value = heir_dip }
					export_to_variable = { which = heirMilVar value = heir_mil }
					change_variable = { which = heirAdmVar which = heirDipVar }
					change_variable = { which = heirAdmVar which = heirMilVar }
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = heirAdmVar value = 9 } }
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = nsc_heir_will_die
		country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.165 days = 180 }

#Heir's Fate
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.165
	title = new_sun_cult.165.t
	desc = { trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = nsc_heir_will_die } } desc = new_sun_cult.165.da }
	desc = { trigger = { has_country_flag = nsc_heir_will_die } desc = new_sun_cult.165.db }
	picture = { trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = nsc_heir_will_die } } picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { has_country_flag = nsc_heir_will_die } picture = DEATH_OF_HEIR_eventPicture }
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Heir come back
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.165.a
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = nsc_heir_will_die } }
		set_heir = kidnapped_heir_@ROOT
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_ruler_flag = was_ruler_when_kidnapping_happened }
				has_regency = no
			}
			custom_tooltip = nsc_ruler_will_step_down_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				set_country_flag = nsc_no_level_loss
				kill_ruler = yes
				add_stability_or_adm_power = yes
			}
		}
		clr_ruler_flag = was_ruler_when_kidnapping_happened
		add_trust = { who = event_target:nsc_target_country value = -25 }
		add_opinion = { who = event_target:nsc_target_country modifier = nsc_suspicious_behaviour_big }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { limit = { has_heir_flag = heir_consort_mage_personality }
				add_ruler_modifier = {
					name = heir_mage_personality_mod
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	#Heir is found dead
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.165.b
		trigger = { has_country_flag = nsc_heir_will_die }
		add_prestige = -5
		clr_country_flag = nsc_heir_will_die
		clr_ruler_flag = was_ruler_when_kidnapping_happened
		add_trust = { who = event_target:nsc_target_country value = -25 }
		add_opinion = { who = event_target:nsc_target_country modifier = nsc_suspicious_behaviour_big }
	}
	
	after = {
		clr_country_flag = nsc_no_level_loss
		event_target:nsc_target_country = {
			set_country_flag = nsc_kidnapping_on_@ROOT
			country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.169 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

#Incident starts for real
#Samartal is announced
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.170
	title = new_sun_cult.170.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.170.d
	picture = GREAT_BUILDING_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_incident_active = incident_summit_of_samartal
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.171 days = 730 }
			clr_country_flag = nsc_assassination_attempt
			clr_country_flag = nsc_kidnapping
			clr_country_flag = nsc_arson
			clr_country_flag = nsc_caravan_raided
			clr_country_flag = nsc_instigated_revolts
			if = { limit = { ai = yes }								#Ai is prevented form declaring new wars
				set_country_flag = nsc_samartal_masquerade
			}
		}
	}
	
	#
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.170.a
		custom_tooltip = nsc_incident_samartal_start_tt
		custom_tooltip = nsc_war_will_be_disabled_tt
		add_stability_or_adm_power = yes
	}
	
	after = {
		clr_country_flag = nsc_assassination_attempt
		clr_country_flag = nsc_kidnapping
		clr_country_flag = nsc_arson
		clr_country_flag = nsc_caravan_raided
		clr_country_flag = nsc_instigated_revolts
		set_global_flag = nsc_summit_of_sammartal_started
	}
}

#Samartal starts soon
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.171
	title = new_sun_cult.171.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.171.d
	picture = DIPLOMACY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_incident_active = incident_summit_of_samartal
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = nsc_samartal_masquerade				#Player can't declare war too now
			set_variable = { which = investigationAgainstVar value = 0 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_global_flag = nsc_explosion_balcony }
					NOT = { has_global_flag = nsc_explosion_dancefloor }
					NOT = { has_global_flag = nsc_explosion_buffet }
				}
				random_list = {
					33 = { set_global_flag = nsc_explosion_balcony }
					33 = { set_global_flag = nsc_explosion_dancefloor }
					33 = { set_global_flag = nsc_explosion_buffet }
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.172 days = 150 }
			set_country_flag = nsc_was_at_samartal
		}
	}
	
	#Send your ruler
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.171.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				variable_arithmetic_trigger = {
					export_to_variable = { which = rulerAdmVar value = ADM }
					export_to_variable = { which = rulerDipVar value = DIP }
					export_to_variable = { which = rulerMilVar value = MIL }
					change_variable = { which = rulerAdmVar which = rulerDipVar }
					change_variable = { which = rulerAdmVar which = rulerMilVar }
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = rulerAdmVar value = 9 } }
				}
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = nsc_wars_are_disabled_tt
		every_war_enemy_country = {
			limit = {
				defensive_war_with = ROOT
				religion = bulwari_sun_cult
			}
			white_peace = ROOT
		}
		set_country_flag = nsc_sent_ruler
		set_ruler_flag = nsc_is_at_samartal
	}
	
	#Send your heir
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.171.b
		trigger = { has_heir = yes heir_age = 15 }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				variable_arithmetic_trigger = {
					export_to_variable = { which = heirAdmVar value = heir_adm }
					export_to_variable = { which = heirDipVar value = heir_dip }
					export_to_variable = { which = heirMilVar value = heir_mil }
					change_variable = { which = heirAdmVar which = heirDipVar }
					change_variable = { which = heirAdmVar which = heirMilVar }
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = heirAdmVar value = 9 } }
				}
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = nsc_wars_are_disabled_tt
		every_war_enemy_country = {
			limit = {
				defensive_war_with = ROOT
				religion = bulwari_sun_cult
			}
			white_peace = ROOT
		}
		set_country_flag = nsc_sent_heir
		set_heir_flag = nsc_is_at_samartal
	}
	
	after = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_free_or_tributary_trigger = no
				overlord = { NOT = { religion = bulwari_sun_cult } }
			}
			overlord = {
				add_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = nsc_refused_to_fight
				}
				country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.300 }
			}
		}

		clr_country_flag = nsc_no_level_loss
		clr_country_flag = nsc_ruler_will_come_back
	}
}

#Da ball
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.172
	title = new_sun_cult.172.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.172.d
	picture = THEATRE_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_incident_active = incident_summit_of_samartal
	}
	
	#Go outside
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.172.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 33 }
		if = { limit = { has_global_flag = nsc_explosion_balcony }
			set_country_flag = nsc_same_room_as_explosion
		}
		else_if = { limit = { has_global_flag = nsc_explosion_dancefloor }
			set_country_flag = nsc_adjacent_room_as_explosion
		}
		else = {
			set_country_flag = nsc_far_from_explosion
		}
	}
	
	#Go to the dancefloor
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.172.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 33 }
		if = { limit = { has_global_flag = nsc_explosion_dancefloor }
			set_country_flag = nsc_same_room_as_explosion
		}
		else_if = { limit = { has_global_flag = nsc_explosion_buffet }
			set_country_flag = nsc_adjacent_room_as_explosion
		}
		else = {
			set_country_flag = nsc_far_from_explosion
		}
	}
	
	#Go to the buffet
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.172.c
		ai_chance = { factor = 33 }
		if = { limit = { has_global_flag = nsc_explosion_buffet }
			set_country_flag = nsc_same_room_as_explosion
		}
		else_if = { limit = { has_global_flag = nsc_explosion_balcony }
			set_country_flag = nsc_adjacent_room_as_explosion
		}
		else = {
			set_country_flag = nsc_far_from_explosion
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.173 days = 1 }
	}
}

#The Tragedy of Samartal
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.173
	title = new_sun_cult.173.t
	desc = { trigger = { has_country_flag = nsc_same_room_as_explosion } desc = new_sun_cult.173.da }
	desc = { trigger = { has_country_flag = nsc_adjacent_room_as_explosion } desc = new_sun_cult.173.db }
	desc = { trigger = { has_country_flag = nsc_far_from_explosion } desc = new_sun_cult.173.dc }
	picture = PLAGUE_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_incident_active = incident_summit_of_samartal
	}
	
	#Ruler/heir died
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.173.a
		trigger = { has_country_flag = nsc_same_room_as_explosion }
		if = { limit = { has_ruler_flag = nsc_is_at_samartal }
			kill_ruler = yes
		}
		else_if = { limit = { has_heir_flag = nsc_is_at_samartal }
			kill_heir = { allow_new_heir = yes }
			reduce_stability_or_adm_power = yes
		}
		else = {
			reduce_stability_or_adm_power = yes
		}
	}
	
	#Ruler/heir severely injured
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.173.b
		trigger = { has_country_flag = nsc_adjacent_room_as_explosion }
		reduce_stability_or_adm_power = yes
	}
	
	#ruler/heir lightly injured
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.173.c
		trigger = { has_country_flag = nsc_far_from_explosion }
		reduce_stability_or_adm_power = yes
	}
	
	after = {
		country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.174 days = 60 }
	}
}

#Aftermath
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.174
	title = new_sun_cult.174.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.174.d
	picture = ACCUSATION_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_incident_active = incident_summit_of_samartal
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = nsc_investigation_starts } }
				set_global_flag = nsc_investigation_starts
				REB = {
					set_variable = { which = nscInvestigationProgressVar value = 0 }
					set_variable = { which = nscLocalInvestigationProgressVar value = 0 }
					set_variable = { which = nscGlobalInvestigationProgress value = 0 }
					set_variable = { which = nscGlobalInvestigationProgressPerCent value = 0 }
				}
				every_country = {
					if = { limit = { has_country_flag = nsc_was_at_samartal }
						country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.177 days = 730 }
					}
					else_if = { limit = { capital_scope = { superregion = bulwar_superregion } }
						country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.194 }
					}
				}
				REB = { set_variable = { which = nscGlobalInvestigationProgress value = 1 } }
				calculate_local_investigation_impact = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	#Dead ruler
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.174.a
		trigger = { has_country_flag = nsc_same_room_as_explosion }
		custom_tooltip = nsc_samartal_investigation_starts_tt
		every_known_country = {
			limit = {
				religion = bulwari_sun_cult
				NOT = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				NOT = { overlord_of = ROOT }
			}
			add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = nsc_tragedy_of_samartal }
			add_trust = { who = ROOT value = -15  }
		}
		hidden_effect = {	#This event is blocked while your ruler is away. Fires it again in case it was blocked
			if = { limit = { has_country_flag = azka_evran_education_event_will_happen }
				country_event = { id = azka_evran.8 days = 365 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	#Injured ruler
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.174.b
		trigger = { has_country_flag = nsc_adjacent_room_as_explosion }
		custom_tooltip = nsc_samartal_investigation_starts_tt
		if = { limit = { has_ruler_flag = nsc_is_at_samartal }
			set_ruler_flag = nsc_injured
			clr_ruler_flag = nsc_is_at_samartal
			custom_tooltip = nsc_ruler_injured_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				if = { limit = { adm = 2 }
					change_adm = -2
					set_ruler_flag = nsc_adm_2
				}
				else_if = { limit = { adm = 1 }
					change_adm = -1
					set_ruler_flag = nsc_adm_1
				}
				if = { limit = { dip = 2 }
					change_dip = -2
					set_ruler_flag = nsc_dip_2
				}
				else_if = { limit = { dip = 1 }
					change_dip = -1
					set_ruler_flag = nsc_dip_1
				}
				if = { limit = { mil = 2 }
					change_mil = -2
					set_ruler_flag = nsc_mil_2
				}
				else_if = { limit = { mil = 1 }
					change_mil = -1
					set_ruler_flag = nsc_mil_1
				}
				add_ruler_modifier = { name = nsc_wounded_ruler duration = 365 }
			}
		}
		else_if = { limit = { has_heir_flag = nsc_is_at_samartal }
			set_heir_flag = nsc_injured
			clr_heir_flag = nsc_is_at_samartal
			custom_tooltip = nsc_heir_injured_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				if = { limit = { heir_adm = 2 }
					change_heir_adm = -2
					set_heir_flag = nsc_adm_2
				}
				else_if = { limit = { heir_adm = 1 }
					change_heir_adm = -1
					set_heir_flag = nsc_adm_1
				}
				if = { limit = { heir_dip = 2 }
					change_heir_dip = -2
					set_heir_flag = nsc_dip_2
				}
				else_if = { limit = { heir_dip = 1 }
					change_heir_dip = -1
					set_heir_flag = nsc_dip_1
				}
				if = { limit = { heir_mil = 2 }
					change_heir_mil = -2
					set_heir_flag = nsc_mil_2
				}
				else_if = { limit = { heir_mil = 1 }
					change_heir_mil = -1
					set_heir_flag = nsc_mil_1
				}
			}
		}
		every_known_country = {
			limit = {
				religion = bulwari_sun_cult
				NOT = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				NOT = { overlord_of = ROOT }
			}
			add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = nsc_tragedy_of_samartal }
			add_trust = { who = ROOT value = -15  }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				50 = { country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.175 days = 365 } }	#Ruler/heir recovers
				50 = { country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.176 days = 365 } }	#Ruler/heir dies
			}
		}
	}
	
	#Healthy ruler
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.174.c
		trigger = { has_country_flag = nsc_far_from_explosion }
		custom_tooltip = nsc_samartal_investigation_starts_tt
		every_known_country = {
			limit = {
				religion = bulwari_sun_cult
				NOT = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				NOT = { overlord_of = ROOT }
			}
			add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = nsc_tragedy_of_samartal }
			add_trust = { who = ROOT value = -15  }
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		clr_country_flag = nsc_no_level_loss
		clr_country_flag = nsc_same_room_as_explosion
		clr_country_flag = nsc_adjacent_room_as_explosion
		clr_country_flag = nsc_far_from_explosion
		set_country_flag = nsc_investigation_enabled
	}
}

		clr_ruler_flag = nsc_dip_1

		clr_ruler_flag = nsc_mil_1
		clr_heir_flag = nsc_adm_2
		clr_heir_flag = nsc_adm_1
		clr_heir_flag = nsc_dip_2
		clr_heir_flag = nsc_dip_1
		clr_heir_flag = nsc_mil_2

#Investigation event chain
#Magical object manufacturer is found
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.177
	title = new_sun_cult.177.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.177.d
	picture = MERCHANTS_TALKING_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_incident_active = incident_summit_of_samartal
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			REB = { set_variable = { which = nscGlobalInvestigationProgressPerCent value = 17 } }
			calculate_local_investigation_impact = yes
			if = { limit = { REB = { check_variable = { which = nscInvestigationProgressVar which = nscInvestigaionBoostUpperThreshold } } } #the variable is the total nb of finished investigation divided by the number of investigable countries
				country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.178 days = 365 }
			}
			else_if = { limit = { REB = { check_variable = { which = nscInvestigationProgressVar which = nscInvestigaionBoostMiddleThreshold } } }
				country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.178 days = 545 }
			}
			else_if = { limit = { REB = { check_variable = { which = nscInvestigationProgressVar which = nscInvestigaionBoostLowerThreshold } } }
				country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.178 days = 730 }
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.178 days = 910 }
			}
			clr_country_flag = nsc_sent_ruler
			clr_country_flag = nsc_sent_heir
		}
	}
	
	#
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.177.a
		custom_tooltip = nsc_investigation_progresses_begining_tt
	}
}

#Perpetrators' leader reveals everything
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.182
	title = new_sun_cult.182.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.182.d
	picture = ADVISOR_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_incident_active = incident_summit_of_samartal
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = nsc_investigation_enabled
			set_variable = { which = PersonallyInvestigatedCountriesVar value = 0 }
			every_known_country = {
				if = { limit = { has_country_flag = nsc_was_investigated_by_@ROOT }
					ROOT = { change_variable = { which = PersonallyInvestigatedCountriesVar value = 1 } }
				}
				clr_country_flag = nsc_is_investigated_by_@ROOT
			}
			nsc_remove_all_investigation_ongoing_modifier = yes
		}
	}
	
	#Make amends
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.182.a
		trigger = { check_variable = { which = PersonallyInvestigatedCountriesVar value = 1 } }
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = PersonallyInvestigatedCountriesVar value = 5 } }
			add_years_of_income = -1
		}
		else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = PersonallyInvestigatedCountriesVar value = 4 } }
			add_years_of_income = -0.8
		}
		else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = PersonallyInvestigatedCountriesVar value = 3 } }
			add_years_of_income = -0.6
		}
		else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = PersonallyInvestigatedCountriesVar value = 2 } }
			add_years_of_income = -0.4
		}
		else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = PersonallyInvestigatedCountriesVar value = 1 } }
			add_years_of_income = -0.2
		}
		every_known_country = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = nsc_was_investigated_by_@ROOT }
			reverse_add_opinion = { who = FROM modifier = nsc_paid_reparations }
			remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = nsc_tragedy_of_samartal }
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = { is_in_war = { attacker_leader = ROOT casus_belli = cb_nsc_investigation } }
			white_peace = ROOT
		}
		set_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_summit_of_samartal value = 0 }
	}
	
	#Don't make amends
	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		name = new_sun_cult.182.b
		every_country = {
			limit = { is_in_war = { attacker_leader = ROOT casus_belli = cb_nsc_investigation } }
			white_peace = ROOT
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.193 days = 30 }
	}
}

#Local Investigation starts (investigator)
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.183
	title = new_sun_cult.183.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.183.d
	picture = DIPLOMACY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Investigators will be assholes
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.183.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		custom_tooltip = nsc_more_chances_to_cause_a_war_tt
		nsc_add_asshole_investigator_modifier = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			random_known_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = nsc_investigation_just_started_by_@ROOT }
				country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.184 }
				country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.186 days = 90 random = 60 }
				country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.187 days = 180 random = 180 }
				country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.186 days = 210 random = 150 }
				clr_country_flag = nsc_investigation_just_started_by_@ROOT
			}
		}
	}
	
	#Investigators will be normal
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.183.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		hidden_effect = {
			random_known_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = nsc_investigation_just_started_by_@ROOT }
				country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.184 }
				country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.186 days = 120 random = 180 }
				country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.186 days = 365 random = 180 }
				clr_country_flag = nsc_investigation_just_started_by_@ROOT
			}
		}
	}
}

#Local Investigation monthly tick
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.185
	title = new_sun_cult.185.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.185.d
	picture = DIPLOMACY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = nsc_investigation_enabled
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = nsc_is_investigated_by_@ROOT
				exists = no
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.185.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					exists = yes
					OR = {
						is_subject = no
						is_subject_of_type = tributary_state_anb
					}
					is_lesser_in_union = no
				}
			}
			if = { limit = { ai = no }
				FROM = {
					change_variable = { which = nscInvestigationOf_@ROOT value = 1 }
					set_variable = { which = nscPerCentInvestigationOf_@ROOT which = nscInvestigationOf_@ROOT }
					divide_variable = { which = nscPerCentInvestigationOf_@ROOT value = 24 }
					multiply_variable = { which = nscPerCentInvestigationOf_@ROOT value = 100 }
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = { limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = nsc_investigation_stopped_@FROM } }
				set_country_flag = nsc_investigation_stopped_@FROM
				if = { limit = { exists = FROM }
					FROM = { clr_country_flag = nsc_is_investigated_by_@ROOT }
				}
				country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.192 }
			}
		}
	}
}

#Nosy Investigators
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.186
	title = new_sun_cult.186.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.186.d
	picture = NOBLE_ESTATE_TAKE_OVER_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		FROM = {
			exists = yes
			OR = {
				is_subject = no
				is_subject_of_type = tributary_state_anb
			}
			is_lesser_in_union = no
		}
		has_country_flag = nsc_investigation_enabled
		has_country_flag = nsc_is_investigated_by_@FROM
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = { nsc_calculate_army_strength_ratio = { who = FROM other_wars_ratio = 0.75 } }
	}
	
	#Bear with them
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.186.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		add_legitimacy = -10
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_intrusive_investigators duration = 9125 }
		add_opinion = { who = FROM modifier = nsc_nosy_investigators }
	}
	
	#Expel them
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.186.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1000
			modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { check_variable = { which = armyStrengthRatio value = 0.4 } } }
			modifier = { factor = 0 calc_true_if = { all_known_country = { war_with = ROOT } amount = 3 } }
			modifier = { factor = 0 any_known_country = { war_with = ROOT war_score_against = { who = ROOT value = 50 } } }
		}
		custom_tooltip = nsc_they_might_declare_war_tt
		add_opinion = { who = FROM modifier = nsc_nosy_investigators }
		reverse_add_opinion = { who = FROM modifier = nsc_expelled_investigators }
		hidden_effect = { 
			clr_country_flag = nsc_is_investigated_by_@FROM
			clr_country_flag = nsc_@FROM_diplomat_sent
			set_country_flag = nsc_has_expelled_@FROM
			FROM = { country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.188 } }
			change_variable = { which = investigationAgainstVar value = -1 }
		}
	}
}

#Expelled Investigators
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.188
	title = new_sun_cult.188.t
	desc = {
		trigger = { NOT = { is_in_war = { casus_belli = cb_nsc_investigation attacker_leader = FROM } } }
		desc = new_sun_cult.188.da
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { is_in_war = { casus_belli = cb_nsc_investigation attacker_leader = FROM } }
		desc = new_sun_cult.188.db
	}
	picture = ACCUSATION_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			nsc_calculate_army_strength_ratio = { who = FROM other_wars_ratio = 0.5 }
			nsc_remove_investigation_ongoing_modifier = yes
		}
	}
	
	#To war
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.188.a
		trigger = { NOT = { is_in_war = { casus_belli = cb_nsc_investigation attacker_leader = FROM } } }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 99
			modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { check_variable = { which = armyStrengthRatio value = 0.5 } } }
			modifier = { factor = 0 FROM = { ai = no } NOT = { check_variable = { which = armyStrengthRatio value = 0.7 } } }
			modifier = { factor = 0 calc_true_if = { all_known_country = { war_with = ROOT } amount = 3 } }
		}
		declare_war_with_cb = { who = FROM casus_belli = cb_nsc_investigation }
		custom_tooltip = nsc_1v1_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { limit = { has_country_flag = nsc_is_investigated_by_@FROM }
				clr_country_flag = nsc_is_investigated_by_@FROM
				FROM = { country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.188 days = 1 } }
			}
			if = { limit = { ai = no FROM = { ai = yes } }
				FROM = { set_country_flag = nsc_was_at_war_with_@ROOT }
			}
			if = { limit = { ai = yes FROM = { ai = no } }
				set_country_flag = nsc_was_at_war_with_@FROM
			}
		}
	}
	
	#We can't
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.188.b
		trigger = { NOT = { is_in_war = { casus_belli = cb_nsc_investigation attacker_leader = FROM } } }
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		add_prestige = -5
	}
	
	#Ok
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.188.c
		trigger = { is_in_war = { casus_belli = cb_nsc_investigation attacker_leader = FROM } }
	}
}

#Incident end
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.193
	title = new_sun_cult.193.t
	desc = { trigger = { incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_summit_of_samartal value = 2 } } desc = new_sun_cult.193.da }
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_summit_of_samartal value = 2 } }
			incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_summit_of_samartal value = -1 }
		}
		desc = new_sun_cult.193.db
	}
	desc = { trigger = { NOT = { incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_summit_of_samartal value = -1 } } } desc = new_sun_cult.193.dc }
	picture = CIVIL_WAR_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_incident_active = incident_summit_of_samartal
	}
	
	#High incident counter
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.193.a
		trigger = { incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_summit_of_samartal value = 2 } }
		end_incident = incident_summit_of_samartal
		increase_nsc_isolation_level = yes
	}
	
	#Medium incident counter
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.193.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_summit_of_samartal value = 2 } }
			incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_summit_of_samartal value = -1 }
		}
		end_incident = incident_summit_of_samartal
	}
	
	#Low incident counter
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.193.c
		trigger = { NOT = { incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_summit_of_samartal value = -1 } } }
		end_incident = incident_summit_of_samartal
		decrease_nsc_isolation_level = yes
	}
	
	after = {
		clr_country_flag = nsc_samartal_masquerade
		clr_country_flag = active_nsc_incident_flag
		clr_country_flag = nsc_was_investigated
		clr_country_flag = nsc_was_at_samartal
		clr_global_flag = nsc_explosion_balcony
		clr_global_flag = nsc_explosion_dancefloor
		clr_global_flag = nsc_explosion_buffet
		clr_global_flag = nsc_investigation_starts
		every_known_country = {
			clr_country_flag = nsc_was_investigated_by_@ROOT
			clr_country_flag = nsc_was_fully_investigated_by_@ROOT
			clr_country_flag = nsc_is_investigated_by_@ROOT
			clr_country_flag = nsc_has_expelled_@ROOT
			clr_country_flag = nsc_was_at_war_with_@ROOT
			ROOT = { clr_country_flag = nsc_investigation_stopped_@PREV }
		}
	}
}

#The Rise of Artificery
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.195
	title = new_sun_cult.195.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.195.d
	picture = BIG_BOOK_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Pass a law to prohibit it
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.195.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = { factor = 5 ruler_has_personality = lawgiver_personality }
		}
		custom_tooltip = nsc_incident_artificery_start_tt
		custom_tooltip = nsc_chosen_role_up_tt
		add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_rise_of_artificery value = -1 }
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_ban_on_artificery duration = -1 desc = nsc_until_incident_end_tt }
	}
	
	#Hard ban
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.195.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = { factor = 100 ruler_has_personality = mage_personality }
			modifier = { factor = 10 ruler_has_personality = lawgiver_personality }
		}
		custom_tooltip = nsc_incident_artificery_start_tt
		custom_tooltip = nsc_much_chosen_role_up_tt
		add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_rise_of_artificery value = -2 }
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_hard_ban_on_artificery duration = -1 desc = nsc_until_incident_end_tt }
	}
	
	#Just advise against it
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.195.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = { factor = 5 ruler_has_personality = free_thinker_personality }
			modifier = { factor = 10 ruler_has_personality = scholar_personality }
			modifier = { factor = 0 ruler_has_personality = mage_personality }
		}
		custom_tooltip = nsc_incident_artificery_start_tt
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_light_ban_on_artificery duration = -1 desc = nsc_until_incident_end_tt }
	}
	
	after = {
		country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.196 days = 365 random = 180 }
	}
}

	}

			modifier = { factor = 5 ruler_has_personality = careful_personality }
			modifier = { factor = 0 ruler_has_personality = mage_personality }

		custom_tooltip = nsc_chosen_role_down_tt
		add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_rise_of_artificery value = 1 }
		add_estate_loyalty = { estate = estate_mages loyalty = -10 }
		add_estate_loyalty = { estate = estate_nobles loyalty = -10 }
	}
	
	after = {
		country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.197 days = 365 random = 180 }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.197
	title = new_sun_cult.197.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.197.d
	picture = ECONOMY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = nsc_duel_null }
	}
	
	#Good idea !
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.197.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 89
			modifier = { factor = 0 is_in_deficit = yes }
			modifier = { factor = 0 ruler_has_personality = greedy_personality }
			modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { num_of_owned_provinces_with = { superregion = bulwar_superregion value = 5 } } }
		}
		custom_tooltip = nsc_excavation_tt
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_excavation_underway duration = -1 desc = nsc_until_incident_end_tt }
	}
	
	#Good idea, here is a mountain of cash
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.197.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = { factor = 0 is_in_deficit = yes }
			modifier = { factor = 0 ruler_has_personality = greedy_personality }
			modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { num_of_owned_provinces_with = { superregion = bulwar_superregion value = 5 } } }
			modifier = { factor = 10 ruler_has_personality = entrepreneur_personality }
		}
		custom_tooltip = nsc_excavation_big_funds_tt
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_great_excavation_underway duration = -1 desc = nsc_until_incident_end_tt }
	}
	
	#Meh. Let's not
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.197.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		add_prestige = -10
	}
	
	after = {
		country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.198 days = 365 random = 180 }
	}
}

#Humans don't like the ban
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.200
	title = new_sun_cult.200.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.200.d
	picture = ANGRY_MOB_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Fuck them up
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.200.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { manpower_percentage = 0.1 } }
			modifier = { factor = 10 ruler_has_personality = cruel_personality }
			modifier = { factor = 100 ruler_has_personality = mage_personality }
		}
		custom_tooltip = nsc_chosen_role_up_tt
		add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_rise_of_artificery value = -1 }
		if = { limit = { num_of_owned_provinces_with = { NOT = { culture = sun_elf } value = 3 } }
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = { 
					NOT = { culture = sun_elf }
					NOT = { has_province_flag = nsc_rebel_spawned }
				}
				spawn_rebels = { type = particularist_rebels size = 1 }
				set_province_flag = nsc_rebel_spawned
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = { 
					NOT = { culture = sun_elf }
					NOT = { has_province_flag = nsc_rebel_spawned }
				}
				spawn_rebels = { type = particularist_rebels size = 1 }
				set_province_flag = nsc_rebel_spawned
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = { 
					NOT = { culture = sun_elf }
					NOT = { has_province_flag = nsc_rebel_spawned }
				}
				spawn_rebels = { type = particularist_rebels size = 1 }
				set_province_flag = nsc_rebel_spawned
			}
		}
		else = {
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_province_flag = nsc_rebel_spawned } }
				spawn_rebels = { type = particularist_rebels size = 1 }
				set_province_flag = nsc_rebel_spawned
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_province_flag = nsc_rebel_spawned } }
				spawn_rebels = { type = particularist_rebels size = 1 }
				set_province_flag = nsc_rebel_spawned
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_province_flag = nsc_rebel_spawned } }
				spawn_rebels = { type = particularist_rebels size = 1 }
				set_province_flag = nsc_rebel_spawned
			}
		}
	}
	
	#Loosen the artificery ban a bit
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.200.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = { factor = 5 ruler_has_personality = free_thinker_personality }
			modifier = { factor = 5 ruler_has_personality = scholar_personality }
			modifier = { factor = 0 ruler_has_personality = mage_personality }
		}
		custom_tooltip = nsc_chosen_role_down_tt
		add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_rise_of_artificery value = 1 }
		if = { limit = { has_country_modifier = nsc_hard_ban_on_artificery }
			remove_country_modifier = nsc_hard_ban_on_artificery
			add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_ban_on_artificery duration = -1 desc = nsc_until_incident_end_tt }
			add_estate_loyalty = { estate = estate_mages loyalty = -10 }
			add_estate_loyalty = { estate = estate_nobles loyalty = -10 }
		}
		else_if = { limit = { has_country_modifier = nsc_ban_on_artificery }
			remove_country_modifier = nsc_ban_on_artificery
			add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_light_ban_on_artificery duration = -1 desc = nsc_until_incident_end_tt }
			add_estate_loyalty = { estate = estate_mages loyalty = -10 }
			add_estate_loyalty = { estate = estate_nobles loyalty = -10 }
		}
		else_if = { limit = { has_country_modifier = nsc_light_ban_on_artificery }
			remove_country_modifier = nsc_light_ban_on_artificery
			add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_no_ban_on_artificery duration = -1 desc = nsc_until_incident_end_tt }
			add_estate_loyalty = { estate = estate_mages loyalty = -10 }
			add_estate_loyalty = { estate = estate_nobles loyalty = -10 }
		}
		random_owned_province = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_province_flag = nsc_rebel_spawned } }
			spawn_rebels = { type = noble_rebels size = 1 }
			set_province_flag = nsc_rebel_spawned
		}
	}
	
	#Loosen the artificery ban a lot
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.200.c
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = nsc_light_ban_on_artificery } }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = { factor = 10 ruler_has_personality = free_thinker_personality }
			modifier = { factor = 10 ruler_has_personality = scholar_personality }
			modifier = { factor = 0 ruler_has_personality = mage_personality }
		}
		custom_tooltip = nsc_much_chosen_role_down_tt
		add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_rise_of_artificery value = 2 }
		if = { limit = { has_country_modifier = nsc_hard_ban_on_artificery }
			remove_country_modifier = nsc_hard_ban_on_artificery
			add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_light_ban_on_artificery duration = -1 desc = nsc_until_incident_end_tt }
			add_estate_loyalty = { estate = estate_mages loyalty = -20 }
			add_estate_loyalty = { estate = estate_nobles loyalty = -20 }
		}
		else_if = { limit = { has_country_modifier = nsc_ban_on_artificery }
			remove_country_modifier = nsc_ban_on_artificery
			add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_no_ban_on_artificery duration = -1 desc = nsc_until_incident_end_tt }
			add_estate_loyalty = { estate = estate_mages loyalty = -20 }
			add_estate_loyalty = { estate = estate_nobles loyalty = -20 }
		}
		random_owned_province = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_province_flag = nsc_rebel_spawned } }
			spawn_rebels = { type = noble_rebels size = 1 }
			set_province_flag = nsc_rebel_spawned
		}
		random_owned_province = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_province_flag = nsc_rebel_spawned } }
			spawn_rebels = { type = noble_rebels size = 1 }
			set_province_flag = nsc_rebel_spawned
		}
	}
	
	#Request them to be patient
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.200.e
		trigger = { 
			OR = {
				ruler_has_personality = charismatic_negotiator_personality
				ruler_has_personality = silver_tongue_personality
				ai = yes
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = { factor = 10 ruler_has_personality = mage_personality }
			modifier = { factor = 5 ruler_has_personality = calm_personality }
			modifier = { factor = 5 ruler_has_personality = careful_personality }
		}
		highlight = yes
		reduce_legitimacy_medium_effect = yes
	}
	
	after = {
		country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.201 days = 365 random = 180 }
		every_owned_province = { clr_province_flag = nsc_rebel_spawned }
	}
}

#Mages provoke artificers
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.201
	title = new_sun_cult.201.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.201.d
	picture = CIVIL_WAR_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					unit_in_siege = no
					unit_in_battle = no
				}
				save_event_target_as = duel_province_target
			}
			capital_scope = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						unit_in_siege = no
						unit_in_battle = no
					}
					save_event_target_as = duel_province_target
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	#bypass for ai
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.201.a
		trigger = { ai = yes }
		random_list = {
			50 = { country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.203 days = 90 } }
			50 = { country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.204 days = 90 } }
		}
	}
	
	#It's time to du-du-du-du- du-du-du-du-du- DUEL !
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.201.b
		goto = duel_province_target
		trigger = { ai = no }
		custom_tooltip = nsc_timetodududu_duel_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:duel_province_target = {
				province_event = { id = new_sun_cult.202 days = 60 }
			}
		}
	}
}

#Duel starts
province_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.202
	title = new_sun_cult.202.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.202.d
	picture = COUNTRY_COLLAPSE_eventPicture
	goto = ROOT
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Mages strike first
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.202.a
		custom_tooltip = nsc_duel_mages_first_tt
		set_province_flag = nsc_duel
		if = { limit = { units_in_province = 1 }
			set_province_flag = nsc_duel_null
		}
		spawn_rebels = { type = mage_duelists_rebels size = 2 }
		spawn_rebels = { type = artificer_duelists_rebels size = 2 }
	}
	
	#Artificers strike first
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.202.b
		custom_tooltip = nsc_duel_artificer_first_tt
		set_province_flag = nsc_duel
		if = { limit = { units_in_province = 1 }
			set_province_flag = nsc_duel_null
		}
		spawn_rebels = { type = artificer_duelists_rebels size = 2 }
		spawn_rebels = { type = mage_duelists_rebels size = 2 }
	}
	
	#Toss a coin
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.202.c
		set_province_flag = nsc_duel
		if = { limit = { units_in_province = 1 }
			set_province_flag = nsc_duel_null
		}
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				spawn_rebels = { type = mage_duelists_rebels size = 2 }
				spawn_rebels = { type = artificer_duelists_rebels size = 2 }
			}
			50 = {
				spawn_rebels = { type = artificer_duelists_rebels size = 2 }
				spawn_rebels = { type = mage_duelists_rebels size = 2 }
			}
		}
	}
}

		}
		disband_rebels = mage_duelists_rebels

						has_country_modifier = nsc_great_excavation_underway
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.206 days = 365 }
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.207 days = 545 }
			}
		}
	}
}
