#Excavation Results
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.206
	title = new_sun_cult.206.t
	desc = { trigger = { has_country_flag = nsc_excavation_successful } desc = new_sun_cult.206.da }
	desc = { trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = nsc_excavation_successful } } desc = new_sun_cult.206.db }
	picture = { trigger = { has_country_flag = nsc_excavation_successful } picture = ECONOMY_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = nsc_excavation_successful } } picture = BANKRUPTCY_eventPicture }
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			FROM = { FROM = { clr_province_flag = nsc_duel_null } }
			if = { limit = { num_of_owned_provinces_with = { superregion = bulwar_superregion value = 5 } }		#Get fucked if you're too small
				if = { limit = { has_country_modifier = nsc_excavation_underway }								#50% chance with the normal excavation modifier
					random_list = {
						50 = {
							random_owned_province = {
								limit = {
									superregion = bulwar_superregion
									NOT = { has_province_flag = nsc_excavation_target }
								}
								set_province_flag = nsc_excavation_target
							}
							set_country_flag = nsc_excavation_successful
						}
						50 = { }
					}
				}
				else = {																						#100% chance with the great excavation modifier
					random_owned_province = {
						limit = {
							superregion = bulwar_superregion
							NOT = { has_province_flag = nsc_excavation_target }
						}
						set_province_flag = nsc_excavation_target
					}
					set_country_flag = nsc_excavation_successful
				}
			}
			if = { limit = { num_of_owned_provinces_with = { superregion = bulwar_superregion value = 30 } }	#Another chance of excavating something if you have a lot of provinces
				if = { limit = { has_country_modifier = nsc_excavation_underway }								#50% chance with the normal excavation modifier
					random_list = {
						50 = {
							random_owned_province = {
								limit = {
									superregion = bulwar_superregion
									NOT = { has_province_flag = nsc_excavation_target }
								}
								set_province_flag = nsc_excavation_target
							}
						}
						50 = { }
					}
					set_country_flag = nsc_excavation_successful
				}
				else = {																						#100% chance with the great excavation modifier
					random_owned_province = {
						limit = {
							superregion = bulwar_superregion
							NOT = { has_province_flag = nsc_excavation_target }
						}
						set_province_flag = nsc_excavation_target
					}
					set_country_flag = nsc_excavation_successful
				}
			}
			if = { limit = { num_of_owned_provinces_with = { superregion = bulwar_superregion value = 60 } }	#Bonus if you're big
				random_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						superregion = bulwar_superregion
						NOT = { has_province_flag = nsc_excavation_target }
					}
					set_province_flag = nsc_excavation_target
				}
				set_country_flag = nsc_excavation_successful
			}
		}
	}
	
	#Give them to the mages
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.206.a
		trigger = { has_country_flag = nsc_excavation_successful }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = { factor = 10 ruler_has_personality = mage_personality }
			modifier = { factor = 5 ruler_has_personality = careful_personality }
		}
		custom_tooltip = nsc_much_chosen_role_up_tt
		add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_rise_of_artificery value = -2 }
		add_estate_loyalty = { estate = estate_mages loyalty = 10 }
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_mage_relics duration = 9125 }
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = { has_province_flag = nsc_excavation_target }
			add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = genie_relics duration = -1 }
		}
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_excavation_underway
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_great_excavation_underway
	}
	
	#Give them to the artificers
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.206.b
		trigger = { has_country_flag = nsc_excavation_successful }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = { factor = 10 ruler_has_personality = free_thinker_personality }
			modifier = { factor = 5 ruler_has_personality = scholar_personality }
			modifier = { factor = 0 ruler_has_personality = mage_personality }
		}
		custom_tooltip = nsc_much_chosen_role_down_tt
		add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_rise_of_artificery value = 2 }
		add_estate_loyalty = { estate = estate_mages loyalty = -10 }
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_artificer_relics duration = 9125 }
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = { has_province_flag = nsc_excavation_target }
			add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = genie_relics duration = -1 }
		}
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_excavation_underway
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_great_excavation_underway
	}
	
	#Share it
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.206.c
		trigger = { has_country_flag = nsc_excavation_successful }
		ai_chance = { factor = 25 }
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_both_relics duration = 9125 }
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = { has_province_flag = nsc_excavation_target }
			add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = genie_relics duration = -1 }
		}
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_excavation_underway
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_great_excavation_underway
	}
	
	#Keep it for yourself
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.206.e
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = { factor = 5 ruler_has_personality = greedy_personality }
			modifier = { factor = 0 NOT = { estate_loyalty = { estate = estate_mages loyalty = 35 } } }
		}
		trigger = { has_country_flag = nsc_excavation_successful }
		add_estate_loyalty = { estate = estate_mages loyalty = -5 }
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = { has_province_flag = nsc_excavation_target }
			add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = genie_relics duration = -1 }
			add_province_modifier = { name = nsc_state_relics duration = 9125 }
		}
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_excavation_underway
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_great_excavation_underway
	}
	
	#Fucking hell
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.206.f
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = nsc_excavation_successful } }
		add_prestige = -5
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_excavation_underway
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_great_excavation_underway
	}
	
	after = {
		clr_country_flag = nsc_excavation_successful
		country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.207 days = 180 }
	}
}

#Incident Outcome
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.207
	title = new_sun_cult.207.t
	desc = { trigger = { incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_rise_of_artificery value = 3 } } desc = new_sun_cult.207.da }
	desc = {
		trigger = {
				NOT = { incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_rise_of_artificery value = 3 } }
				incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_rise_of_artificery value = -2 }
		}
		desc = new_sun_cult.207.db
	}
	desc = { trigger = { NOT = { incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_rise_of_artificery value = -2 } } } desc = new_sun_cult.207.dc }
	picture = { trigger = { incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_rise_of_artificery value = 3 } } picture = ELECTION_REPUBLICAN_eventPicture }
	picture = {
		trigger = {
				NOT = { incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_rise_of_artificery value = 3 } }
				incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_rise_of_artificery value = -2 }
		}
		picture = TRADEGOODS_eventPicture
	}
	picture = { trigger = { NOT = { incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_rise_of_artificery value = -2 } } } picture = THEATRE_eventPicture }
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Artificery for everyone
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.207.a
		trigger = { incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_rise_of_artificery value = 3 } } 				#max possible -7
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_conceded_artificery duration = -1 }
		decrease_nsc_isolation_level = yes
		custom_tooltip = nsc_artificery_enabled_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = artificery_unlocked }
				}
				country_event = {
					id = magic_artificery_setup.1
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
		end_incident = incident_rise_of_artificery
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = estate_organization.5 days = 35 } }		#choose organization for artificer estate
	}
	
	#Artificery for Elves only
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.207.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_rise_of_artificery value = 3 } }
			incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_rise_of_artificery value = -2 }
		}
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_restricted_artificery duration = -1 }
		custom_tooltip = nsc_artificery_semi_enabled_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = artificery_unlocked }
				}
				country_event = {
					id = magic_artificery_setup.1
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = nsc_sun_elf_artificery
		end_incident = incident_rise_of_artificery
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = estate_organization.5 days = 35 } }		#choose organization for artificer estate
	}
	
	#Artificery Banned
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.207.c
		trigger = { NOT = { incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_rise_of_artificery value = -2 } } }	#min possible +9
		set_country_flag = nsc_banned_artificery
		increase_nsc_isolation_level = yes
		custom_tooltip = nsc_artificery_banned_tt
		if = { limit = { has_estate = estate_mages }
			if = { limit = { has_estate_privilege = estate_mages_battlemage_academies }
				remove_estate_privilege = estate_mages_battlemage_academies
			}
			set_estate_privilege = estate_mages_empowered_mages
		}
		end_incident = incident_rise_of_artificery
	}
	
	after = {
		clr_country_flag = active_nsc_incident_flag
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_ban_on_artificery
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_hard_ban_on_artificery
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_light_ban_on_artificery
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_no_ban_on_artificery
		set_country_flag = had_nsc_incident_flag
	}
}

#Ravelian preachers have come to our land
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.210
	title = new_sun_cult.210.t
	desc = { trigger = { has_country_flag = nsc_lucian_carter_in_our_lands } desc = new_sun_cult.210.da }
	desc = { trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = nsc_lucian_carter_in_our_lands } } desc = new_sun_cult.210.db }
	desc = { 
		trigger = { 
			NOT = { has_country_flag = nsc_lucian_carter_in_our_lands }
			capital_scope = { 
				OR = {
					continent= south_america
					continent = north_america
				}
			}
		}
		desc =  new_sun_cult.210.daelantir
	}
	picture = PIETY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Reject them
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.210.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 45
			modifier = { factor = 5 isolationism = 3 }
		}
		custom_tooltip = nsc_incident_ravelianism_start_tt
		custom_tooltip = nsc_chosen_role_up_tt
		add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_spread_of_ravelianism value = 1 }
		add_legitimacy = 10
	}
	
	#Leave them be
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 45
		}
		name = new_sun_cult.210.b
		custom_tooltip = nsc_incident_ravelianism_start_tt
		add_prestige = 5
	}
	
	#Invite them to the court
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.210.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = { factor = 5 NOT = { isolationism = 2 } }
			modifier = { factor = 5 NOT = { isolationism = 1 } }
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_vassal = yes
				overlord = { religion = bulwari_sun_cult }
				NOT = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = nsc_incident_ravelianism_start_tt
		custom_tooltip = nsc_chosen_role_down_tt
		add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_spread_of_ravelianism value = -1 }
		if = { limit = { has_country_flag = nsc_lucian_carter_in_our_lands }
			define_advisor = {
				type = theologian
				name = "Lucian Carter"
				skill = 3
				culture = anbenncoster
				religion = ravelian
				discount = yes
			}
		}
		else = {
			define_advisor = {
				type = theologian
				skill = 2
				culture = anbenncoster
				religion = ravelian
				discount = yes
			}
		}
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_ravelian_at_court duration = 3650 }
	}
	
	after = {
		country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.211 days = 545 random = 180 }
	}
}

#Missionaries arrive in the capital 
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.211
	title = new_sun_cult.211.t
	desc = { 
		trigger = { 
			capital_scope = { 
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						continent= south_america
						continent = north_america
					}
				}
			}
		}
		desc = new_sun_cult.211.d
	}
	desc = { 
		trigger = { 
			capital_scope = { 
				OR = {
					continent= south_america
					continent = north_america
				}
			}
		}
		desc =  new_sun_cult.211.daelantir
	}
	picture = STREET_SPEECH_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Ruler wants to hear them
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.211.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = { factor = 5 NOT = { isolationism = 2 } }
			modifier = { factor = 5 NOT = { isolationism = 1 } }
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_vassal = yes
				overlord = { religion = bulwari_sun_cult }
				NOT = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = nsc_much_chosen_role_down_tt
		add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_spread_of_ravelianism value = -3 }
		random_list = {
			33 = { change_adm = 1 }
			33 = { change_dip = 1 }
			33 = { change_mil = 1 }
		}
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_ravelian_influence duration = 3650 }
	}
	
	#Let them chill
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.211.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 45
		}
		custom_tooltip = nsc_chosen_role_down_tt
		add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_spread_of_ravelianism value = -2 }
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_ravelian_influence duration = 3650 }
	}
	
	#Sounds like it's expulsion time
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.211.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 45
			modifier = { factor = 5 isolationism = 3 }
		}
		custom_tooltip = nsc_chosen_role_up_tt
		add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_spread_of_ravelianism value = 1 }
		add_stability_or_adm_power = yes
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_expelled_ravelian_missionaries duration = 3650 }
	}
	
	after = {
		if = { limit = { owns = 600 }												#.212 only happens if you own Azanerdu
			country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.212 days = 545 random = 180 }
			country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.213 days = 1095 random = 365 }
		}
		else = {
			country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.213 days = 545 random = 180 }
		}
	}
}

#Ravelian traders want to establish a trading community
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.213
	title = new_sun_cult.213.t
	desc = { 
		trigger = { 
			capital_scope = { 
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						continent= south_america
						continent = north_america
					}
				}
			}
		}
		desc = new_sun_cult.213.d
	}
	desc = { 
		trigger = { 
			capital_scope = { 
				OR = {
					continent= south_america
					continent = north_america
				}
			}
		}
		desc =  new_sun_cult.213.daelantir
	}
	picture = NAVAL_MILITARY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_province = { save_event_target_as = ravelian_province }
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = { NOT = { religion = ravelian } }
				save_event_target_as = ravelian_province
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					capital_scope = {
						NOT = { religion = ravelian }
						superregion = bulwar_superregion
					}
				}
				capital_scope = { save_event_target_as = ravelian_province }
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { religion = ravelian }
					province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1
					development = 10
				}
				save_event_target_as = ravelian_province
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { religion = ravelian }
					province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1
					development = 20
				}
				save_event_target_as = ravelian_province
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { religion = ravelian }
					province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1
					development = 30
				}
				save_event_target_as = ravelian_province
			}
		}
	}
	
	#allow it
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.213.a
		goto = ravelian_province
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = { factor = 2 NOT = { isolationism = 2 } }
			modifier = { factor = 5 NOT = { isolationism = 1 } }
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_vassal = yes
				overlord = { religion = bulwari_sun_cult }
				NOT = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = nsc_much_chosen_role_down_tt
		add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_spread_of_ravelianism value = -2 }
		random_list = {
			33 = { change_adm = 1 }
			33 = { change_dip = 1 }
			33 = { change_mil = 1 }
		}
		event_target:ravelian_province = { add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = nsc_ravelian_society duration = -1 } }
	}
	
	#refuse this time
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.213.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 45
			modifier = { factor = 5 isolationism = 3 }
		}
		custom_tooltip = nsc_chosen_role_up_tt
		add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_spread_of_ravelianism value = 1 }
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_kept_control_of_trade duration = 3650 }
		event_target:ravelian_province = { set_province_flag = denied_ravelian_society }
	}
	
	#refuse for good
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.213.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 45
			modifier = { factor = 2 isolationism = 3 }
			modifier = { factor = 5 isolationism = 4 }
		}
		custom_tooltip = nsc_much_chosen_role_up_tt
		custom_tooltip = nsc_ravelian_communities_disabled_tt
		add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_spread_of_ravelianism value = 4 }
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_kept_control_of_trade duration = 3650 }
		set_country_flag = nsc_banned_ravelian_communities
	}
	
	after = {
		country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.216 days = 730 random = 180 }
		country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.214 days = 180 random = 180 }
		country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.214 days = 365 random = 180 }
		country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.214 days = 545 random = 180 }
		country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.214 days = 730 random = 180 }
		country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.214 days = 910 random = 180 }
		country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.214 days = 1095 random = 180 }
		country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.214 days = 1275 random = 180 }
	}
}

#Ravelian society
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.214
	title = new_sun_cult.214.t
	desc = { 
		trigger = { 
			capital_scope = { 
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						continent= south_america
						continent = north_america
					}
				}
			}
		}
		desc = new_sun_cult.214.d
	}
	desc = { 
		trigger = { 
			capital_scope = { 
				OR = {
					continent= south_america
					continent = north_america
				}
			}
		}
		desc =  new_sun_cult.214.daelantir
	}
	picture = REFORM_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = nsc_banned_ravelian_communities }
		any_owned_province = {
			development = 10
			NOT = { religion = ravelian }
			NOT = { has_province_modifier = nsc_ravelian_society }
			NOT = { has_province_flag = denied_ravelian_society }
			NOT = { has_province_flag = nsc_current_target }
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					development = 10
					NOT = { religion = ravelian }
					NOT = { has_province_modifier = nsc_ravelian_society }
					NOT = { has_province_flag = denied_ravelian_society }
					NOT = { has_province_flag = nsc_current_target }
				}
				save_event_target_as = ravelian_province
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					development = 10
					NOT = { religion = ravelian }
					NOT = { has_province_modifier = nsc_ravelian_society }
					NOT = { has_province_flag = denied_ravelian_society }
					NOT = { has_province_flag = nsc_current_target }
					province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1
				}
				save_event_target_as = ravelian_province
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					development = 20
					NOT = { religion = ravelian }
					NOT = { has_province_modifier = nsc_ravelian_society }
					NOT = { has_province_flag = denied_ravelian_society }
					NOT = { has_province_flag = nsc_current_target }
					province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1
				}
				save_event_target_as = ravelian_province
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					development = 30
					NOT = { religion = ravelian }
					NOT = { has_province_modifier = nsc_ravelian_society }
					NOT = { has_province_flag = denied_ravelian_society }
					NOT = { has_province_flag = nsc_current_target }
					province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1
				}
				save_event_target_as = ravelian_province
			}
			event_target:ravelian_province = { set_province_flag = nsc_current_target }
		}
	}
	
	#cool
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.214.a
		goto = ravelian_province
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = { factor = 2 NOT = { isolationism = 2 } }
			modifier = { factor = 5 NOT = { isolationism = 1 } }
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_vassal = yes
				overlord = { religion = bulwari_sun_cult }
				NOT = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = nsc_chosen_role_down_tt
		add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_spread_of_ravelianism value = -1 }
		event_target:ravelian_province = { add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = nsc_ravelian_society duration = -1 } }
	}
	
	#ban them
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.214.b
		goto = ravelian_province
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = { factor = 2 isolationism = 3 }
			modifier = { factor = 5 isolationism = 4 }
		}
		custom_tooltip = nsc_chosen_role_up_tt
		add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_spread_of_ravelianism value = 1 }
		event_target:ravelian_province = { set_province_flag = denied_ravelian_society }
	}
	
	after = {
		event_target:ravelian_province = { clr_province_flag = nsc_current_target }
		if = { limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = nsc_society_raided } }
			country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.215 days = 365 random = 180 }
		}
		else = {
			random = { 
				chance = 25
				country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.215 days = 365 random = 180 }
			}
		}
	}
}

#Ravelian society raided
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.215
	title = new_sun_cult.215.t
	desc = { 
		trigger = { 
			capital_scope = { 
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						continent= south_america
						continent = north_america
					}
				}
			}
		}
		desc = new_sun_cult.215.d
	}
	desc = { 
		trigger = { 
			capital_scope = { 
				OR = {
					continent= south_america
					continent = north_america
				}
			}
		}
		desc =  new_sun_cult.215.daelantir
	}
	picture = RELIGIOUS_TURMOIL_eventPicture
	goto = raided_province
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		any_owned_province = {
			NOT = { religion = ravelian }
			NOT = { has_province_flag = nsc_current_target }
			has_province_modifier = nsc_ravelian_society
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { religion = ravelian }
					has_province_modifier = nsc_ravelian_society
				}
				save_event_target_as = raided_province
			}
			event_target:ravelian_province = { set_province_flag = nsc_current_target }
		}
	}
	
	#Investigate
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.215.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = { factor = 2 NOT = { isolationism = 2 } }
			modifier = { factor = 5 NOT = { isolationism = 1 } }
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_vassal = yes
				overlord = { religion = bulwari_sun_cult }
				NOT = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = nsc_chosen_role_down_tt
		add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_spread_of_ravelianism value = -1 }
		add_adm_power = -50
	}
	
	#Don't give a shit
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.215.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
			modifier = { factor = 2 isolationism = 3 }
			modifier = { factor = 5 isolationism = 4 }
		}
		custom_tooltip = nsc_chosen_role_up_tt
		add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_spread_of_ravelianism value = 1 }
		event_target:ravelian_province = {
			add_devastation = 25
			remove_province_modifier = nsc_ravelian_society
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		set_country_flag = nsc_society_raided
		event_target:ravelian_province = { clr_province_flag = nsc_current_target }
	}
}

#Rectorate invites you
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.217
	title = new_sun_cult.217.t
	desc = { 
		trigger = { 
			capital_scope = { 
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						continent= south_america
						continent = north_america
					}
				}
			}
		}
		desc = new_sun_cult.217.d
	}
	desc = { 
		trigger = { 
			capital_scope = { 
				OR = {
					continent= south_america
					continent = north_america
				}
			}
		}
		desc =  new_sun_cult.217.daelantir
	}
	picture = FEAST_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Send a big delegation - with heir
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.217.a
		trigger = { has_heir = yes heir_age = 15 }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = { factor = 2 NOT = { isolationism = 2 } }
			modifier = { factor = 5 NOT = { isolationism = 1 } }
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_vassal = yes
				overlord = { religion = bulwari_sun_cult }
				NOT = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = nsc_much_chosen_role_down_tt
		custom_tooltip = nsc_send_heir_away_tt
		add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_spread_of_ravelianism value = -3 }
		add_years_of_income = -0.5
		add_prestige = 15
		if = {
			limit = { has_ruler_modifier = heir_mage_personality_mod }
			set_country_flag = exiled_heir_mage
		}
		exile_heir_as = exiled_heir_@ROOT
		hidden_effect = {
			set_ruler_flag = was_ruler_when_heir_left
			set_country_flag = nsc_sent_heir
			random_list = {
				50 = { country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.218 days = 365 random = 60 } }			#Cube speaks
				50 = { country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.219 days = 365 random = 60 } }			#Cube doesn't give a shit about you
			}
		}
	}
	
	#Send a big delegation - without heir
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.217.b
		trigger = { OR = { has_heir = no NOT = { heir_age = 15 } } }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = { factor = 2 NOT = { isolationism = 2 } }
			modifier = { factor = 5 NOT = { isolationism = 1 } }
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_vassal = yes
				overlord = { religion = bulwari_sun_cult }
				NOT = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = nsc_much_chosen_role_down_tt
		add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_spread_of_ravelianism value = -3 }
		add_years_of_income = -0.5
		add_prestige = 15
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				50 = { country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.218 days = 365 random = 60 } }			#Cube speaks
				50 = { country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.219 days = 365 random = 60 } }			#Cube doesn't give a shit about you
			}
		}
	}
	
	#Send a moderate delegation
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.217.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
		}
		custom_tooltip = nsc_chosen_role_down_tt
		add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_spread_of_ravelianism value = -2 }
		add_years_of_income = -0.2
		add_prestige = 5
		hidden_effect = { 
			random_list = {
				50 = { country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.218 days = 365 random = 60 } }			#Cube speaks
				50 = { country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.219 days = 365 random = 60 } }			#Cube doesn't give a shit about you
			}
		}
	}
	
	#Don't go
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.217.e
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = { factor = 10 isolationism = 4 }
		}
		custom_tooltip = nsc_much_chosen_role_up_tt
		add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_spread_of_ravelianism value = 3 }
		every_known_country = {
			limit = { religion = ravelian }
			add_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = nsc_refused_rectorate_invitation }
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.220 days = 365 } }
	}
}

#The Cube has spoken !
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.218
	title = new_sun_cult.218.t
	desc = { 
		trigger = { 
			capital_scope = { 
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						continent= south_america
						continent = north_america
					}
				}
			}
		}
		desc = new_sun_cult.218.d
	}
	desc = { 
		trigger = { 
			capital_scope = { 
				OR = {
					continent= south_america
					continent = north_america
				}
			}
		}
		desc =  new_sun_cult.218.daelantir
	}
	picture = TRADE_GOODS_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Awesome
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.218.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = { factor = 2 NOT = { isolationism = 2 } }
			modifier = { factor = 5 NOT = { isolationism = 1 } }
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_vassal = yes
				overlord = { religion = bulwari_sun_cult }
				NOT = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = nsc_much_chosen_role_down_tt
		add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_spread_of_ravelianism value = -3 }
		add_prestige = 25
		if = { limit = { has_country_flag = nsc_sent_heir }
			set_heir = exiled_heir_@ROOT
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = exiled_heir_mage }
				set_heir_mage_effect = yes
				clr_country_flag = exiled_heir_mage
			}
			set_heir_religion = ravelian
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_ruler_flag = was_ruler_when_heir_left }
					has_regency = no
				}
				custom_tooltip = nsc_ruler_will_step_down_tt
				hidden_effect = {
					set_country_flag = nsc_no_level_loss
					kill_ruler = yes
					add_stability_or_adm_power = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	#Sounds like bullshit
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.218.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = { factor = 0.5 NOT = { stability = 0 } }
			modifier = { factor = 2 isolationism = 3 }
			modifier = { factor = 5 isolationism = 4 }
		}
		custom_tooltip = nsc_much_chosen_role_up_tt
		if = { limit = { has_country_flag = nsc_sent_heir }
			custom_tooltip = nsc_heir_is_banned_tt
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = exiled_heir_mage }
				clr_country_flag = exiled_heir_mage
			}
		}
		add_incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_spread_of_ravelianism value = 2 }
		reduce_stability_or_adm_power = yes
	}
	
	after = {
		clr_country_flag = nsc_sent_heir
		clr_country_flag = nsc_no_level_loss
		clr_ruler_flag = was_ruler_when_heir_left
		country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.220 days = 365 }
	}
}

#Incident Outcome
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.220
	title = new_sun_cult.220.t
	desc = { 
		trigger = { 
			capital_scope = { 
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						continent= south_america
						continent = north_america
					}
				}
			}
			incident_variable_value = { 
				incident = incident_spread_of_ravelianism 
				value = 4 
			} 
		} 
		desc = new_sun_cult.220.da 
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			capital_scope = { 
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						continent= south_america
						continent = north_america
					}
				}
			}
			NOT = { 
				incident_variable_value = { 
					incident = incident_spread_of_ravelianism 
					value = 4 
				} 
			}
			incident_variable_value = { 
				incident = incident_spread_of_ravelianism 
				value = -4 
			}
		}
		desc = new_sun_cult.220.db
	}
	desc = { 
		trigger = { 
			capital_scope = { 
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						continent= south_america
						continent = north_america
					}
				}
			}
			NOT = { 
				incident_variable_value = { 
					incident = incident_spread_of_ravelianism 
					value = -4 
				} 
			} 
		} 
		desc = new_sun_cult.220.dc 
	}
	desc = { 
		trigger = { 
			capital_scope = { 
				OR = {
					continent= south_america
					continent = north_america
				}
			}
			incident_variable_value = { 
				incident = incident_spread_of_ravelianism 
				value = 4 
			} 
		} 
		desc = new_sun_cult.220.daaelantir
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			capital_scope = { 
				OR = {
					continent= south_america
					continent = north_america
				}
			}
			NOT = { 
				incident_variable_value = { 
					incident = incident_spread_of_ravelianism 
					value = 4 
				} 
			}
			incident_variable_value = { 
				incident = incident_spread_of_ravelianism 
				value = -4 
			}
		}
		desc = new_sun_cult.220.dbaelantir
	}
	desc = { 
		trigger = { 
			capital_scope = { 
				OR = {
					continent= south_america
					continent = north_america
				}
			}
			NOT = { 
				incident_variable_value = { 
					incident = incident_spread_of_ravelianism 
					value = -4 
				} 
			} 
		} 
		desc = new_sun_cult.220.dcaelantir
	}

	picture = { trigger = { incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_spread_of_ravelianism value = 4 } } picture = WESTERNIZATION_eventPicture }
	picture = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_spread_of_ravelianism value = 4 } }
			incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_spread_of_ravelianism value = -4 }
		}
		picture = PIETY_eventPicture
	}
	picture = { trigger = { NOT = { incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_spread_of_ravelianism value = -4 } } } picture = PRAYING_eventPicture }
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Ravelianism defeated
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.220.a
		trigger = { incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_spread_of_ravelianism value = 4 } } 				#max possible -6
		increase_nsc_isolation_level = yes
		if = { limit = { any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = nsc_ravelian_society } }
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = { has_province_modifier = nsc_ravelian_society }
				change_religion = ravelian
				remove_province_modifier = nsc_ravelian_society
			}
		}
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_ravelianism_defeated duration = 9125 }
		end_incident = incident_spread_of_ravelianism
	}
	
	#Significant ravelian presence
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.220.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_spread_of_ravelianism value = 4 } }
			incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_spread_of_ravelianism value = -4 }
		}
		if = { limit = { any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = nsc_ravelian_society } }
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = { has_province_modifier = nsc_ravelian_society }
				change_religion = ravelian
				add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = "religious_zeal_at_conv" duration = 9125 }
				remove_province_modifier = nsc_ravelian_society
			}
		}
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_significant_ravelian_presence duration = 9125 }
		end_incident = incident_spread_of_ravelianism
	}
	
	#Strong ravelian presence
	#Let's convert!
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.220.c
		trigger = { NOT = { incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_spread_of_ravelianism value = -4 } } }	#min possible +7
		change_religion = ravelian
		add_country_modifier = { name = "conversion_zeal" duration = 3650 }
		if = { limit = { any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = nsc_ravelian_society } }
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = { has_province_modifier = nsc_ravelian_society }
				change_religion = ravelian
				add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = "religious_zeal_at_conv" duration = 9125 }
				remove_province_modifier = nsc_ravelian_society
			}
		}
		end_incident = incident_spread_of_ravelianism
	}
	
	#Fuck that
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.220.e
		trigger = { NOT = { incident_variable_value = { incident = incident_spread_of_ravelianism value = -4 } } }	#min possible +7
		decrease_nsc_isolation_level = yes
		if = { limit = { any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = nsc_ravelian_society } }
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = { has_province_modifier = nsc_ravelian_society }
				change_religion = ravelian
				add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = "religious_zeal_at_conv" duration = 9125 }
				remove_province_modifier = nsc_ravelian_society
			}
		}
		add_prestige = 10
		reduce_stability_or_adm_power = yes
		end_incident = incident_spread_of_ravelianism
	}
	
	after = {
		clr_country_flag = active_nsc_incident_flag
		clr_country_flag = nsc_banned_ravelian_communities
		clr_country_flag = nsc_society_raided
		clr_country_flag = nsc_lucian_carter_in_our_lands
		clr_country_flag = nsc_lucian_carter_happened
		every_owned_province = { clr_province_flag = denied_ravelian_society }
		set_country_flag = had_nsc_incident_flag
	}
}

#Starter Event
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.242
	title = new_sun_cult.242.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.242.d
	picture = EXPLORERS_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #Send messengers to the Szal-Fazil
		name = new_sun_cult.242.a
		
		add_legitimacy = 10
		add_republican_tradition = 3
		add_devotion = 10

		}

	}

			discount = yes
		}

		add_estate_influence_modifier = {
			estate = estate_church
			desc = nsc_protected_szal_fazil
			influence = -10
			duration = 7300
		}
		add_prestige = -10

			}
		add_estate_loyalty = { estate = estate_church loyalty = -10 }
		add_estate_influence_modifier = {

		}

					NOT = { has_reform = states_general_reform }
				} 
				country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.249 days = 400 random = 150 } #Magic Heir
			}
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.244 days = 360 random = 180 } }

#Seat of the Magi
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.246
	title = new_sun_cult.246.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.246.d
	picture = ST_PETERS_CHURCH_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = { 
					culture = sun_elf
					NOT = { province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1 }
					NOT = { has_terrain = farmlands }
				}
				save_event_target_as = nsc_elven_mage_hogwarts_target
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = { 
					culture = sun_elf
					has_terrain = farmlands
					NOT = { province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1 }
				}
				save_event_target_as = nsc_elven_nobility_hogwarts_target
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = { province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1 }
				save_event_target_as = nsc_cot_mage_hogwarts_target
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = { 
					culture_group = bulwari
					development = 15
					NOT = { province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1 }
				}
				save_event_target_as = nsc_human_burgher_hogwarts_target
				set_province_flag = nsc_nsc_human_burgher_hogwarts_province
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = { 
					culture_group = bulwari
					has_terrain = drylands
					NOT = { province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1 }
				}
				save_event_target_as = nsc_human_mage_hogwarts_target
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = { 
					culture_group = bulwari
					has_terrain = drylands
					NOT = { province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1 }
					NOT = { has_province_flag = nsc_nsc_human_burgher_hogwarts_province }
				}
				save_event_target_as = nsc_human_mage_hogwarts_target
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Elven Mage
		name = new_sun_cult.246.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = nsc_bulwari_organization }
			any_owned_province = {
				culture = sun_elf
				NOT = { province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1 }
				NOT = { has_terrain = farmlands }
				has_saved_event_target = nsc_elven_mage_hogwarts_target
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = nsc_chosen_role_up_tt
		custom_tooltip = nsc_increase_magi_influence
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = nsc_magi_supported_magi
			duration = 3650
		}
		event_target:nsc_elven_mage_hogwarts_target = {
			add_building_construction = {
				building = mage_tower
				speed = 0.5
				cost = 0.5
			}
		add_province_modifier = { name = nsc_bulwari_hogwarts duration = -1 }
		}
		set_country_flag = nsc_privilege_magi_influence
	}
	
	option = { #Elven Nobility
		name = new_sun_cult.246.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = nsc_bulwari_organization }
			any_owned_province = {
				culture = sun_elf
				has_terrain = farmlands
				NOT = { province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1 }
				has_saved_event_target = nsc_elven_nobility_hogwarts_target
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = nsc_chosen_role_up_tt
		custom_tooltip = nsc_increase_noble_influence
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = nsc_magi_supported_nobles
			duration = 3650
		}
		add_estate_influence_modifier = {
			estate = estate_nobles
			desc = nsc_hogwarts_in_elven_nobles_prov
			influence = 10
			duration = 20
		}

				speed = 0.5

#Final Event
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.247
	title = new_sun_cult.247.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.247.d
	picture = REFORM_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #Now we have mages!
		name = new_sun_cult.247.a
		end_incident = incident_teachings_szal_fazil
		if = { limit = { has_country_flag = nsc_szal_fazil_evocation }
			increase_nsc_isolation_level = yes
		}
		else_if = { limit = { has_country_flag = nsc_szal_fazil_abjuration }
			increase_nsc_isolation_level = yes
		}
		else_if = { limit = { has_country_flag = nsc_szal_fazil_transmutation }
		}
		else_if = { limit = { has_country_flag = nsc_szal_fazil_divination }
			decrease_nsc_isolation_level = yes
		}
		else_if = { limit = { has_country_flag = nsc_szal_fazil_conjuration }
			decrease_nsc_isolation_level = yes
		}
		custom_tooltip = nsc_enable_mage_estate_tt
	}
	
	after = {
		clr_country_flag = nsc_human_country_magic_prohibition
		clr_country_flag = active_nsc_incident_flag
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.248 days = 10 } }
	}
}

#Hidden event for the privileges
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.248
	title = new_sun_cult.248.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.248.d
	picture = PRAYING_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes
	
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.248.a
		
		if = { limit = { has_country_flag = nsc_szal_fazil_evocation }
			set_estate_privilege = estate_mages_organization_jaherian_statute
			set_estate_privilege = estate_mages_sun_elf_evocation
		}
		else_if = { limit = { has_country_flag = nsc_szal_fazil_abjuration }

			set_estate_privilege = estate_mages_organization_jaherian_statute
			set_estate_privilege = estate_mages_sun_elf_abjuration
		}
		else_if = { limit = { has_country_flag = nsc_szal_fazil_transmutation }
			set_estate_privilege = estate_mages_organization_jaherian_statute
			set_estate_privilege = estate_mages_syncretic_transmutation
		}
		else_if = { limit = { has_country_flag = nsc_szal_fazil_divination }
			set_estate_privilege = estate_mages_organization_jaherian_statute
			set_estate_privilege = estate_mages_bulwari_divination
		}
		else_if = { limit = { has_country_flag = nsc_szal_fazil_conjuration }
			set_estate_privilege = estate_mages_organization_jaherian_statute
			set_estate_privilege = estate_mages_bulwari_conjuration
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		set_country_flag = had_nsc_incident_flag
		clr_country_flag = nsc_teachings_szal_fazil_started
		clr_country_flag = nsc_people_want_mages
		clr_country_flag = nsc_protected_amman_magi
		clr_country_flag = nsc_bulwari_organization
		clr_country_flag = nsc_tutelage_organization
		clr_country_flag = nsc_syncretic_organization
	}
}

#Assasination attempt
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.250
	title = new_sun_cult.250.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.250.d
	picture = ANGRY_MOB_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = { 
					has_tax_building_trigger = yes
				}
				save_event_target_as = nsc_temple_mob
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.250.a
		
		add_stability = -1
		add_legitimacy = -5
		if = {
			limit = { has_saved_event_target = nsc_temple_mob }
			event_target:nsc_temple_mob = {
				spawn_rebels = {
					type = leadered_peasant_rebels
					size = 2
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			capital_scope = {
				spawn_rebels = {
					type = leadered_peasant_rebels
					size = 2
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.250.b
		
		if = { 
			limit = { has_saved_event_target = nsc_temple_mob }
			event_target:nsc_temple_mob = {
				if = { limit = { has_building = temple } remove_building = temple }
				else = { remove_building = cathedral }
				add_devastation = 15
			}
		}
		else = { capital_scope = { add_devastation = 15 } }
		add_estate_loyalty = { estate = estate_church loyalty = -10 }
	}
}

#Neighbor Sun Elf demands
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.251
	title = new_sun_cult.251.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.251.d
	picture = BORDER_TENSION_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		any_neighbor_country = {
			NOT = { alliance_with = ROOT }
			religion = bulwari_sun_cult
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_neighbor_country = {
				limit = { NOT = { alliance_with = ROOT } religion = bulwari_sun_cult }
				save_event_target_as = nsc_elven_neighbor
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.251.a
		
		reverse_add_opinion = {
			who = event_target:nsc_elven_neighbor
			modifier = nsc_bad_refuse_stop_teaching_magic
		}
		add_prestige = 15
		add_legitimacy = 10
		add_republican_tradition = 3
		add_devotion = 10
	}
	
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.251.b
		
		reverse_add_opinion = {
			who = event_target:nsc_elven_neighbor
			modifier = nsc_good_refuse_stop_teaching_magic
		}
		add_prestige = -10
		add_legitimacy = -10
		add_republican_tradition = -3
		add_devotion = -10
	}
}

#--------# Silent as the Grave #--------#

#Adventurers Dnd Campaign event chain
#Start - Damestar meteorite fall
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.255
	title = damestear.4.t	#this is right title, not a bug
	desc = damestear.4.d
	picture = COMET_SIGHTED_eventPicture
	goto = damestear_province

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		ai = no
		is_year = 1600
		religion = bulwari_sun_cult
		suran_river = { type = all country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		num_of_owned_provinces_with = { province_group = amussus_grave_surroundings value = 6 }
		num_of_owned_provinces_with = { superregion = bulwar_superregion value = 120 }
		is_incident_active = no
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					province_group = amussus_grave_surroundings
					NOT = { province_id = 6101 }
					NOT = { province_id = 6102 }
					NOT = { province_id = 6104 }
					is_city = yes
					NOT = {
						trade_goods = precursor_relics
						trade_goods = damestear
						trade_goods = gold
						has_province_flag = has_damestear
					}
				}
				save_event_target_as = damestear_province
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
        name = damestear.4.a
        ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		event_target:damestear_province = {
			add_base_tax = -2
			add_base_production = -2
			add_base_manpower = -2
			change_trade_goods = damestear
			set_province_flag = has_damestear
			set_province_flag = permanent_damestear
			add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = damestear_rich_deposit duration = -1 }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:damestear_province = { province_event = { id = new_sun_cult.256 days = 5475 random = 3650 } }
			country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.257 days = 365 }
		}
	}
}

#Incident really starts
#Amussu Awakens
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.265
	title = new_sun_cult.265.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.265.d
	picture = AMUSSU_AWAKENS_ANIMATED_eventPicture
	goto = amussu_province_goto
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					province_group = amussus_grave_surroundings
					superregion = bulwar_superregion
				}
				save_global_event_target_as = amussu_province_target
				save_event_target_as = amussu_province_goto
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.265.a
		custom_tooltip = nsc_amussu_incident_starts_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:amussu_province_target = {
				add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = nsc_amussu_province duration = -1 desc = nsc_until_incident_end_tt }
			}
			6106 = { add_province_triggered_modifier = amussu_incident_monthly_pulse }	#Amussu's grave wasteland
			save_global_event_target_as = nsc_incident_target
			set_country_flag = nsc_has_amussu_incident
			set_country_flag = nsc_amussu_has_0_relics
			REB = { 
				set_variable = { which = amussuPowerVar value = 40 }	#only used for loc and tooltips
				set_variable = { which = amussuNbRelicsVar value = 0 }	#only used for loc and tooltips
			}
			nsc_set_relic_provinces_effect = yes
			nsc_set_next_relic_target_effect = yes
		}
		amussus_grave_surroundings = { add_devastation = 30 }
		REB = { set_country_flag = nsc_amussu_invulnerable }
		country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.267 days = 60 }	#First calamity
	}
}

#Amussu finds a relic
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.266
	title = new_sun_cult.266.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.266.d
	picture = EXPLORERS_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	hidden = yes
	
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.266.a
		if = { limit = { REB = { is_variable_equal = { which = amussuNbRelicsVar value = 0 } } }
			country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.269 }	#Second calamity
		}
		else_if = { limit = { REB = { is_variable_equal = { which = amussuNbRelicsVar value = 1 } } }
			country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.271 }	#Third calamity
		}
		else_if = { limit = { REB = { is_variable_equal = { which = amussuNbRelicsVar value = 2 } } }
			country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.276 }	#Fourth calamity
		}
		else_if = { limit = { REB = { is_variable_equal = { which = amussuNbRelicsVar value = 3 } } }
			country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.278 }	#Fifth calamity
		}
		else_if = { limit = { REB = { is_variable_equal = { which = amussuNbRelicsVar value = 4 } } }
			country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.282 }	#Last Relic Found
		}
		REB = { 
			change_variable = { which = amussuNbRelicsVar value = 1 }
			change_variable = { which = amussuPowerVar value = 20 }
		}
	}
}

#First calamity - The Bloody Suran
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.267
	title = new_sun_cult.267.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.267.d
	picture = PLAGUE_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			REB = {
				set_country_flag = nsc_amussu_invulnerable
				set_variable = { which = numOfCalamities value = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.267.a
		custom_tooltip = nsc_amussu_power_increase_tt
		custom_tooltip = nsc_amussu_invulnerable_tt
		custom_tooltip = nsc_bloody_suran_tt
		suran_river = {
			limit = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
			add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = nsc_bloody_suran duration = -1 desc = nsc_until_end_of_calamity_tt }
		}
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_first_calamity_modifier duration = -1 desc = nsc_until_end_of_calamity_tt }
		set_country_flag = nsc_first_calamity
	}
}

#First calamity ends
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.268
	title = new_sun_cult.268.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.268.d
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = { REB = { change_variable = { which = numOfCalamities value = -1 } } }
	}
	
	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = nsc_first_calamity
		suran_river = {
			type = all
			OR = {
				NOT = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
				NOT = { has_province_modifier = nsc_bloody_suran }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.268.a
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_first_calamity_modifier
		if = { limit = { REB = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = numOfCalamities value = 1 } } } }
			custom_tooltip = nsc_amussu_not_invulnerable_tt
			REB = { clr_country_flag = nsc_amussu_invulnerable }
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = nsc_amussu_still_invulnerable_tt
		}
		clr_country_flag = nsc_first_calamity
	}
}

#Fourth calamity - The Thousand Beasts
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.276
	title = new_sun_cult.276.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.276.d
	picture = TRAILS_BASILISK_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			REB = {
				set_country_flag = nsc_amussu_invulnerable
				change_variable = { which = numOfCalamities value = 1 }
				set_variable = { which = numOfBeasts value = 0 }
			}
			event_target:amussu_province_target = {
				every_neighbor_province = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_province_flag = nsc_calamities_rebels_spawned }
						country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT
						REB = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = numOfBeasts value = 11 } } }
					}
					random_list = {
						66 = { spawn_rebels = { type = amussu_calamities_rebels size = 1 } change_controller = REB }
						33 = { spawn_rebels = { type = amussu_calamities_rebels size = 2 } change_controller = REB }
					}
					set_province_flag = nsc_calamities_rebels_spawned
					REB = { change_variable = { which = numOfBeasts value = 1 } }
					every_neighbor_province = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { has_province_flag = nsc_calamities_rebels_spawned }
							country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT
						REB = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = numOfBeasts value = 11 } } }
						}
						random_list = {
							66 = { spawn_rebels = { type = amussu_calamities_rebels size = 1 } change_controller = REB }
							33 = { spawn_rebels = { type = amussu_calamities_rebels size = 2 } change_controller = REB }
						}
						set_province_flag = nsc_calamities_rebels_spawned
						REB = { change_variable = { which = numOfBeasts value = 1 } }
						every_neighbor_province = {
							limit = {
								NOT = { has_province_flag = nsc_calamities_rebels_spawned }
								country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT
								REB = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = numOfBeasts value = 11 } } }
							}
							random_list = {
								66 = { spawn_rebels = { type = amussu_calamities_rebels size = 1 } change_controller = REB }
								33 = { spawn_rebels = { type = amussu_calamities_rebels size = 2 } change_controller = REB }
							}
							set_province_flag = nsc_calamities_rebels_spawned
							REB = { change_variable = { which = numOfBeasts value = 1 } }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			bulwar_superregion = { clr_province_flag = nsc_calamities_rebels_spawned }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.276.a
		custom_tooltip = nsc_amussu_power_increase_tt
		custom_tooltip = nsc_amussu_invulnerable_tt
		custom_tooltip = nsc_thousand_beasts_tt
		set_country_flag = nsc_fourth_calamity
	}
}

#Fifth calamity - Skyfall
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.278
	title = new_sun_cult.278.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.278.d
	picture = COMET_SIGHTED_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			REB = {
				set_country_flag = nsc_amussu_invulnerable
				change_variable = { which = numOfCalamities value = 1 }
			}
			set_variable = { which = numOfArtefactProvinces value = 10 }
			set_variable = { which = numOfWorkingArtefacts value = 0 }
			while = { limit = { check_variable = { which = numOfArtefactProvinces value = 1 } }
				random_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						province_group = amussus_relics_spawns
						NOT = { has_province_flag = nsc_possible_artefact }
						NOT = { has_province_flag = nsc_amussu_relic_province }
					}
					set_province_flag = nsc_possible_artefact
					if = { limit = { ROOT = { check_variable = { which = numOfArtefactProvinces value = 6 } } }
						set_province_flag = nsc_working_artefact
					}
				}
				change_variable = { which = numOfArtefactProvinces value = -1 }
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					province_group = amussus_relics_spawns
					NOT = { has_province_flag = nsc_skyfalled }
				}
				save_event_target_as = nsc_skyfalled_target_1
				set_province_flag = nsc_skyfalled
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					province_group = amussus_relics_spawns
					NOT = { has_province_flag = nsc_skyfalled }
				}
				save_event_target_as = nsc_skyfalled_target_2
				set_province_flag = nsc_skyfalled
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					province_group = amussus_relics_spawns
					NOT = { has_province_flag = nsc_skyfalled }
				}
				save_event_target_as = nsc_skyfalled_target_3
				set_province_flag = nsc_skyfalled
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.278.a
		custom_tooltip = nsc_amussu_power_increase_tt
		custom_tooltip = nsc_amussu_invulnerable_tt
		custom_tooltip = nsc_skyfall_tt
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_fifth_calamity_modifier duration = -1 desc = nsc_until_end_of_calamity_tt }
		event_target:nsc_skyfalled_target_1 = {
			add_devastation = 25
			add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = nsc_small_damestear_deposit duration = 9125 }
		}
		event_target:nsc_skyfalled_target_2 = {
			add_devastation = 25
			add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = nsc_small_damestear_deposit duration = 9125 }
		}
		event_target:nsc_skyfalled_target_3 = {
			add_devastation = 25
			add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = nsc_small_damestear_deposit duration = 9125 }
		}
		set_country_flag = nsc_fifth_calamity
		set_country_flag = nsc_digging_artifacts
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.279 days = 60 random = 60 }
			country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.279 days = 150 random = 60 }
			country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.279 days = 240 random = 60 }
			country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.279 days = 330 random = 60 }
		}
	}
}

#Meteorite falls
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.279
	title = new_sun_cult.279.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.279.d
	picture = COMET_SIGHTED_eventPicture
	goto = nsc_skyfalled_target_1
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = nsc_fifth_calamity
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					superregion = bulwar_superregion
					NOT = { has_province_flag = nsc_skyfalled }
				}
				save_event_target_as = nsc_skyfalled_target_1
				set_province_flag = nsc_skyfalled
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.279.a
		event_target:nsc_skyfalled_target_1 = {
			add_devastation = 25
			add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = nsc_small_damestear_deposit duration = 9125 }
		}
	}
}

#Fifth calamity - finding genie-binding artefacts
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.280
	title = new_sun_cult.280.t
	desc = { trigger = { event_target:nsc_possible_artefact_target = { has_province_flag = nsc_working_artefact } } desc = new_sun_cult.280.da }
	desc = { trigger = { event_target:nsc_possible_artefact_target = { NOT = { has_province_flag = nsc_working_artefact } } } desc = new_sun_cult.280.db }
	picture = { trigger = { event_target:nsc_possible_artefact_target = { has_province_flag = nsc_working_artefact } } picture = SWORD_OF_OSMAN_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { event_target:nsc_possible_artefact_target = { NOT = { has_province_flag = nsc_working_artefact } } } picture = OVEREXTENSION_eventPicture }
	goto = nsc_possible_artefact_target
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { limit = { event_target:nsc_possible_artefact_target = { has_province_flag = nsc_working_artefact } }
				change_variable = { which = numOfWorkingArtefacts value = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	#Found a working artefact
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.280.a
		trigger = { event_target:nsc_possible_artefact_target = { has_province_flag = nsc_working_artefact } }
		custom_tooltip = nsc_gathered_a_working_artifact_tt
		if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = numOfWorkingArtefacts value = 5 } }
			clr_country_flag = nsc_digging_artifacts
			set_country_flag = nsc_using_artifacts
		}
		event_target:nsc_possible_artefact_target = { clr_province_flag = nsc_working_artefact }
	}
	
	#Found a fucked artefact
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.280.b
		trigger = { event_target:nsc_possible_artefact_target = { NOT = { has_province_flag = nsc_working_artefact } } }
		add_prestige = -1
	}
}

		if = { limit = { NOT = { num_of_units_in_province = { who = REB amount = 1 } } }
			random_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = nsc_has_amussu_incident }
				set_country_flag = nsc_beat_amussu
				country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.287 }
			}
		}
		else_if = { limit = { REB = { had_country_flag = { flag = nsc_amussu_last_relic days = 180 } } }
			random_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = nsc_has_amussu_incident }
				country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.287 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			random_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = nsc_has_amussu_incident }
				country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.286 }
			}
		}
		owner = {
			disband_rebels = amussu_main_rebels
		}
	}
}

#Incident end
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.287
	title = new_sun_cult.287.t
	desc = { trigger = { has_country_flag = nsc_beat_amussu } desc = new_sun_cult.287.da }
	desc = { trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = nsc_beat_amussu } } desc = new_sun_cult.287.de }
	picture = { trigger = { has_country_flag = nsc_beat_amussu } picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture }
	picture = { trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = nsc_beat_amussu } } picture = PLAGUE_eventPicture }
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = nsc_has_amussu_incident
		REB = { NOT = { has_country_flag = nsc_amussu_battle_ongoing } }
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = nsc_has_amussu_incident
			bulwar_superregion = {
				limit = { has_province_modifier = nsc_amussu_province }
				save_event_target_as = amussu_modifier_target
			}
			6106 = { remove_province_triggered_modifier = amussu_incident_monthly_pulse }
		}
	}
	
	#Win + Wish to be worshipped as a God-King
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.287.a
		trigger = { has_country_flag = nsc_beat_amussu }
		end_incident = incident_silent_as_the_grave
		if = { limit = { is_chosen_country = yes }
			increase_nsc_isolation_level = yes
		}
		else = {
			decrease_nsc_isolation_level = yes
		}
		add_stability_or_adm_power = yes
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_god_king_wish duration = -1 }
		if = { limit = { REB = { check_variable = { which = amussuNbRelicsVar value = 1 } } }
			country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.288 }
		}
	}
	
	#Win + Wish to oversee a prosperous realm
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.287.b
		trigger = { has_country_flag = nsc_beat_amussu }
		end_incident = incident_silent_as_the_grave
		add_stability_or_adm_power = yes
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_prosperity_wish duration = -1 }
		if = { limit = { REB = { check_variable = { which = amussuNbRelicsVar value = 1 } } }
			country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.288 }
		}
	}
	
	#Win + Wish to ensure all my subjects rise
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.287.c
		trigger = { has_country_flag = nsc_beat_amussu }
		end_incident = incident_silent_as_the_grave
		if = { limit = { is_chosen_country = yes }
			decrease_nsc_isolation_level = yes
		}
		else = {
			increase_nsc_isolation_level = yes
		}
		add_stability_or_adm_power = yes
		add_country_modifier = { name = nsc_subjects_wish duration = -1 }
		if = { limit = { REB = { check_variable = { which = amussuNbRelicsVar value = 1 } } }
			country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.288 }
		}
	}
	
	#loss
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.287.e
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = nsc_beat_amussu } }
		end_incident = incident_silent_as_the_grave
		custom_tooltip = nsc_relics_lost_tt
		reduce_stability_or_adm_power = yes
		event_target:amussu_modifier_target = {
			add_devastation = 100
			add_base_tax = -2
			add_base_production = -2
			add_base_manpower = -2
			set_province_flag = nsc_amussu_devastation
			every_neighbor_province = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_province_flag = nsc_amussu_devastation } }
				add_devastation = 75
				add_base_tax = -1
				add_base_production = -1
				add_base_manpower = -1
				set_province_flag = nsc_amussu_devastation
				every_neighbor_province = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_province_flag = nsc_amussu_devastation } }
					add_devastation = 50
					set_province_flag = nsc_amussu_devastation
				}
				every_neighbor_province = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_province_flag = nsc_amussu_devastation } }
					add_devastation = 25
					set_province_flag = nsc_amussu_devastation
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		clr_country_flag = nsc_first_calamity
		clr_country_flag = nsc_second_calamity
		clr_country_flag = nsc_third_calamity
		clr_country_flag = nsc_fourth_calamity
		clr_country_flag = nsc_using_artifacts
		clr_country_flag = nsc_beat_amussu
		clr_country_flag = nsc_amussu_battle_refused
		clr_country_flag = nsc_amussu_has_0_relics
		clr_country_flag = nsc_amussu_has_1_relics
		clr_country_flag = nsc_amussu_has_2_relics
		clr_country_flag = nsc_amussu_has_3_relics
		clr_country_flag = nsc_amussu_has_4_relics
		clr_country_flag = nsc_amussu_has_5_relics
		clr_country_flag = nsc_relic_A_picked
		clr_country_flag = nsc_relic_B_picked
		clr_country_flag = nsc_relic_C_picked
		clr_country_flag = nsc_relic_D_picked
		clr_country_flag = nsc_relic_E_picked
		clr_country_flag = nsc_relic_F_picked
		clr_country_flag = nsc_relic_G_picked
		clr_country_flag = nsc_relic_H_picked
		clr_country_flag = nsc_relic_I_picked
		clr_country_flag = nsc_relic_J_picked
		REB = {
			clr_country_flag = nsc_amussu_last_relic
			clr_country_flag = nsc_amussu_invulnerable
		}
		clr_country_flag = nsc_gather_gems
		clr_country_flag = nsc_gather_glass
		clr_country_flag = nsc_gather_damestear
		clr_country_flag = nsc_dispel_the_eclipse
		clr_country_flag = nsc_amussu_moves_info_deactivated
		if = {
			limit = { has_saved_global_event_target = amussu_province_target }
			clear_global_event_target = amussu_province_target
		}
		bulwar_superregion = {
			clr_province_flag = nsc_amussu_relic_province
			clr_province_flag = nsc_skyfalled
			remove_province_modifier = nsc_amussu_province
			remove_province_modifier = nsc_bloody_suran
			clr_province_flag = nsc_possible_artefact
			clr_province_flag = nsc_working_artefact
			clr_province_flag = nsc_amussu_relic_province_1
			clr_province_flag = nsc_amussu_relic_province_2
			clr_province_flag = nsc_amussu_relic_province_3
			clr_province_flag = nsc_amussu_relic_province_4
			clr_province_flag = nsc_amussu_relic_province_5
			clr_province_flag = nsc_relic_A
			clr_province_flag = nsc_relic_B
			clr_province_flag = nsc_relic_C
			clr_province_flag = nsc_relic_D
			clr_province_flag = nsc_relic_E
			clr_province_flag = nsc_relic_F
			clr_province_flag = nsc_relic_G
			clr_province_flag = nsc_relic_H
			clr_province_flag = nsc_relic_I
			clr_province_flag = nsc_relic_J
			clr_province_flag = nsc_amussu_devastation
		}
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_first_calamity_modifier
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_third_calamity_modifier

			10 = { trigger = { ruler_has_personality = infertile_personality } remove_ruler_personality = infertile_personality }
			10 = { trigger = { ruler_has_personality = drunkard_personality } remove_ruler_personality = drunkard_personality }
			10 = { trigger = { ruler_has_personality = sinner_personality } remove_ruler_personality = sinner_personality }
			10 = { trigger = { ruler_has_personality = greedy_personality } remove_ruler_personality = greedy_personality }
			10 = { trigger = { ruler_has_personality = cruel_personality } remove_ruler_personality = cruel_personality }
			10 = { trigger = { ruler_has_personality = naive_personality } remove_ruler_personality = naive_personality }
			10 = { trigger = { ruler_has_personality = craven_personality } remove_ruler_personality = craven_personality }
			10 = { trigger = { ruler_has_personality = loose_lips_personality } remove_ruler_personality = loose_lips_personality }
			10 = { trigger = { ruler_has_personality = obsessive_perfectionist_personality } remove_ruler_personality = obsessive_perfectionist_personality }
			10 = { trigger = { ruler_has_personality = malevolent_personality } remove_ruler_personality = malevolent_personality }
		}
	}
}

#Use Dagger of Derumasil
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.291
	title = new_sun_cult.291.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.291.d
	picture = SWORD_OF_OSMAN_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#sacrifice heir
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.291.a
		trigger = { has_heir = yes }
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_dagger_derumasil
		kill_heir = { allow_new_heir = no }
		event_target:nsc_dagger_target = { kill_ruler = yes }
	}
	
	#sacrifice consort
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.291.b
		trigger = { has_consort = yes }
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_dagger_derumasil
		remove_consort_effect = yes
		event_target:nsc_dagger_target = { kill_ruler = yes }
	}
	
	#go back
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.291.c
	}
	
	after = {
		clr_country_flag = nsc_dagger_derumasil_menu
	}
}

#Use Kazam's Keys
country_event = {
	id = new_sun_cult.292
	title = new_sun_cult.292.t
	desc = new_sun_cult.292.d
	picture = SIEGE_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = { define_kazam_siege = yes }
	}
	
	#go back
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.292.a
		highlight = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		name = new_sun_cult.292.b
		trigger = { has_saved_event_target = kazam1 }
		goto = kazam1
		event_target:kazam1 = {
			change_controller = ROOT
			hidden_effect = { province_event = { id = new_sun_cult.293 } }
		}
		remove_country_modifier = nsc_kazam_keys
	}
	
	option = {

	}
